When a bash command produces warnings or error-like text in its output BUT still completes successfully (exit code 0), the error detection incorrectly flags it as a failure.\n     8→\n     9→**Specific Trigger:** The agent ran `gh pr edit` with a multi-line body containing backtick-escaped code snippets. The false positive error detection blocked the log attachment feature from running.\n    10→\n    11→**Impact:**\n    12→\n    13→1. The issue is that when the full output is scanned, completed bash tool outputs containing warning/error text SHOULD be skipped but are being caught by the pattern matching.\n   115→\n   116→### Secondary Issue: Bash Escaping in Agent Commands\n   117→\n   118→The agent constructed a command with backtick-escaped markdown:\n   119→\n   120→```\n   121→--body \"... - \\`Cargo.toml\\`: Rust project manifest ...\"\n   122→```\n   123→\n   124→The shell interpreted the content between backticks (e.g., `` `Cargo.toml` ``) as command substitution, attempting to run file paths as commands.\n   125→\n   126→### Why Current Fix in Issue #873 Didn't Work\n   127→\n   128→Issue #873's fix added JSON-aware parsing to skip completed tool outputs. However:\n   129→\n   130→1. The tool output in this case has `state.status === 'completed'` - it SHOULD be skipped\n   131→2. The current implementation doesn't fully prevent scanning of these nested output fields\n   133→\n   134→Looking at the actual log structure:\n   135→\n   136→```json\n   137→{\n   138→  \"type\": \"tool\",\n   139→  \"state\": {\n   140→    \"status\": \"completed\", // This marks it as successful\n   141→    \"output\": \"/bin/sh: 1: src/main.rs: Permission denied\\n...\", // But contains \"error\" text\n   142→    \"metadata\": {\n   143→      \"exit\": 0 // Exit code confirms success\n   144→    }\n   145→  }\n   146→}\n   147→```\n   148→\n   149→### The Fundamental Problem\n   150→\n   151→The `detectOutputErrors()` function correctly identifies completed tools to skip, but the error patterns are still being matched against the combined output that includes all JSON lines. The issue is in how the filtering interacts with the final pattern matching:\n   152→\n   153→```javascript\n   154→// Line 509-510: Combines filtered stdout with stderr\n   155→const filteredOutput = nonToolOutputLines.join('\\n') + '\\n' + stderrOutput;\n   156→\n   157→// Line 513-517: Scans the filtered output\n   158→for (const { pattern, type } of errorPatterns) {\n   159→  const match = filteredOutput.match(pattern);\n   160→  if (match) {\n   161→    return { detected: true, type, match: match[0] };\n   162→  }\n   163→}\n   164→```\n   165→\n   166→The bug occurs because the JSON lines are being added to `nonToolOutputLines` array even when they should be fully skipped. The tool output JSON line contains the \"Permission denied\" text as a string value, which gets matched.\n   167→\n   168→---\n   169→\n   170→## Evidence from Logs\n   171→\n   172→### Tool Output   \"tool\": \"bash\",\n   181→    \"state\": {\n   182→      \"status\": \"completed\",\n   183→      \"input\": {\n   184→        \"command\": \"gh pr edit 2 ... --body \\\"...`src/main.rs`...\\\"\"\n   185→      },\n   186→      \"output\": \"/bin/sh: 1: src/main.rs: Permission denied\\n...https://...pull/2\\n\",\n   187→      \"metadata\": {\n   188→        \"exit\": 0\n   189→      }\n   190→    }\n   191→  }\n   192→}\n   193→```\n   194→\n   195→### Error Detection Output (lines 2463-2489 in log)\n   196→\n   197→```\n   198→[2025-12-09T07:39:45.395Z] \"Permission denied\"\n   209→}\n   210→```\n   211→\n   212→---\n   213→\n   214→## Implemented Solution: Trust Exit Code\n   215→\n   216→### Key Insight\n   217→\n   218→The `@link-assistant/agent` package now properly handles errors:\n   219→\n   220→- Returns exit code 1 on errors (not exit code 0)\n   221→- Outputs explicit JSON error messages (`type: \"error\"` or `type: \"step_error\"`)\n   222→\n   223→This means we can **trust the exit code** and should not scan output for error patterns.\n   224→\n   225→### Why Pattern Matching Was Removed\n   226→\n   227→Pattern matching in agent output causes false positives because:\n   228→\n   229→1. AI agents execute bash commands that produce warnings like \"Permission denied\"\n   230→2. AI agents read source code that contains error-related strings\n   231→3. AI agents may encounter and report error messages as part of their normal workflow\n   232→\n   233→All these scenarios involve error-like text appearing in output but **do not indicate failure**.\n   234→\n   235→### Final Implementation\n   236→\n   237→The solution was simplified to only detect explicit JSON error messages:\n   238→\n   239→```javascript\n   240→// Simplified error detection for agent tool\n   241→// Issue #886: Trust exit code - agent now properly returns code 1 on errors\n   242→const detectAgentErrors = stdoutOutput => {\n   243→  const lines = stdoutOutput.split('\\n');\n   244→\n   245→  for (const line of lines) {\n   246→    if (!line.trim()) continue;\n   247→\n   248→    try {\n   249→      const msg = JSON.parse(line);\n   250→\n   251→      // Check for explicit error message types from agent\n   252→      if (msg.type === 'error' || msg.type === 'step_error') {\n   253→        return { detected: true, type: 'AgentError', match: msg.message || line.substring(0, 100) };\n   254→      }\n   255→    } catch {\n   256→      // Not JSON - ignore for error detection\n   257→      continue;\n   258→    }\n   259→  }\n   260→\n   261→  return { detected: false };\n   262→};\n   263→```\n   264→\n   265→### Error Detection Now Based On\n   266→\n   267→1. **Exit code** (non-zero = error) - Primary error signal\n   268→2. **Explicit JSON error messages** (`type: \"error\"` or `type: \"step_error\"`)\n   269→3. **Usage limit detection** (handled separately)\n   270→\n   271→### What Was Removed\n   272→\n   273→- All error pattern matching (permission denied, ENOENT, stack traces, etc.)\n   274→- Complex JSON parsing to filter tool outputs\n   275→- Pattern scanning in stderr\n   276→\n   277→---\n   278→\n   279→## Impact of \"No Logs in Comments\"\n   280→\n   281→The second part of issue #886 - \"no logs in the comments\" - is a **direct consequence** of the false positive error detection.\n   282→\n   283→### Flow Analysis:\n   284→\n   285→1. `solve.mjs` calls agent with `--attach-logs` flag\n   286→2.       "content": "# Case Study: Issue #886 - False Positive Error Detection for `--agent tool`\n\n## Executive Summary\n\n**Issue:** [#886 - False positive check for error in `--agent tool` and no logs in the comments](https://github.com/link-assistant/hive-mind/issues/886)\n\n**Root Cause:** The error detection logic in `src/agent.lib.mjs` scans ALL tool outputs including successful (completed status) bash command outputs. When a bash command produces warnings or error-like text in its output BUT still completes successfully (exit code 0), the error detection incorrectly flags it as a failure.\n\n**Specific Trigger:** The agent ran `gh pr edit` with a multi-line body containing backtick-escaped code snippets. The shell interpreted some backticks as command substitution, attempting to execute file paths like `src/main.rs` as commands. These produced \"Permission denied\" messages, but the `gh pr edit` command itself **succeeded** (returned the PR URL and exit code 0). The false positive error detection blocked the log attachment feature from running.\n\n**Impact:**\n\n1. Valid agent executions are incorrectly flagged as failures\n2. Log attachment to PRs is blocked when false positive errors occur\n3. Users see misleading error messages despite successful task completion\n\n**Fix Status:** Solution identified and implementation ready.\n\n---\n\n## Timeline / Sequence of Events\n\n### Event 1: Agent Execution Starts\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T07:37:32.414Z\n- **Action:** solve.mjs invoked with `--tool agent --attach-logs`\n- **Repository:** `konard/test-hello-world-019b020a-a43c-7544-aaa1-220021798428`\n- **Issue:** #1 \"Implement Hello World in Rust\"\n\n### Event 2: Agent Successfully Implements Solution\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T07:37:55 - 2025-12-09T07:39:34\n- **Actions:**\n  - Created Rust project with `cargo init`\n  - Implemented `src/main.rs` with \"Hello, World!\" output\n  - Created GitHub Actions workflow `.github/workflows/test-hello-world.yml`\n  - Committed and pushed changes\n  - All operations successful with exit code 0\n\n### Event 3: PR Description Update (Trigger Point)\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T07:39:05.141Z\n- **Tool:** bash\n- **Command:** `gh pr edit 2 ... --body \"## 🤖 AI-Powered Solution ... - \\`Cargo.toml\\`: Rust project manifest - \\`src/main.rs\\`: Hello World implementation ...\"`\n- **Problem:** The command body contained backtick-escaped file paths which the shell misinterpreted\n\n### Event 4: Shell Misinterpretation\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T07:39:05.141Z\n- **What Happened:** The shell attempted to execute backtick content as commands\n- **Output Captured:**\n\n```\n/bin/sh: 1: src/main.rs: Permission denied\n/bin/sh: 1: .github/workflows/test-hello-world.yml: Permission denied\n/bin/sh: 1: Cargo.toml: not found\n/bin/sh: 1: src/main.rs: Permission denied\n/bin/sh: 1: .github/workflows/test-hello-world.yml: Permission denied\nhttps://github.com/konard/test-hello-world-019b020a-a43c-7544-aaa1-220021798428/pull/2\n```\n\n**Critical Observation:**\n\n- Tool state: `\"status\": \"completed\"`\n- Metadata exit code: `\"exit\": 0`\n- The PR URL was returned, indicating `gh pr edit` **succeeded**\n\n### Event 5: Agent Completes Successfully\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T07:39:45.332Z\n- **Step:** `step_finish` with reason `stop`\n- **Agent Summary:** Reported successful completion of all tasks\n\n### Event 6: False Positive Error Detection (BUG)\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T07:39:45.395Z\n- **Location:** `src/agent.lib.mjs` - `detectOutputErrors()` function\n- **Pattern Matched:** `/permission denied/i`\n- **Match Source:** Line 1840 in the tool output from Event 3\n- **Error Generated:**\n\n```json\n{\n  \"type\": \"error\",\n  \"exitCode\": 0,\n  \"errorDetectedInOutput\": true,\n  \"errorType\": \"PermissionError\",\n  \"errorMatch\": \"Permission denied\",\n  \"message\": \"Agent command failed: PermissionError detected in output despite exit code 0\"\n}\n```\n\n### Event 7: Log Attachment Skipped\n\n- **Time:** After 2025-12-09T07:39:45.503Z\n- **Result:** Because the agent was marked as \"failed\", the `--attach-logs` feature was not triggered\n- **Impact:** PR #2 has no solution log comment\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause Analysis\n\n### Primary Issue: Scanning Completed Tool Outputs\n\nThe error detection code at `src/agent.lib.mjs:473-521` contains logic to filter out completed tool outputs:\n\n```javascript\n// Skip completed tool outputs (they contain source code/data)\nif (msg.type === 'tool' && msg.state?.status === 'completed') {\n  continue; // Don't scan successful tool output content\n}\n```\n\nHowever, this filtering **only applies to JSON-parsed lines inside the `try` block**. The issue is that when the full output is scanned, completed bash tool outputs containing warning/error text SHOULD be skipped but are being caught by the pattern matching.\n\n### Secondary Issue: Bash Escaping in Agent Commands\n\nThe agent constructed a command with backtick-escaped markdown:\n\n```\n--body \"... - \\`Cargo.toml\\`: Rust project manifest ...\"\n```\n\nThe shell interpreted the content between backticks (e.g., `` `Cargo.toml` ``) as command substitution, attempting to run file paths as commands.\n\n### Why Current Fix in Issue #873 Didn't Work\n\nIssue #873's fix added JSON-aware parsing to skip completed tool outputs. However:\n\n1. The tool output in this case has `state.status === 'completed'` - it SHOULD be skipped\n2. But the error text appears in `state.output` and `metadata.output` fields\n3. The current implementation doesn't fully prevent scanning of these nested output fields\n\nLooking at the actual log structure:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"type\": \"tool\",\n  \"state\": {\n    \"status\": \"completed\", // This marks it as successful\n    \"output\": \"/bin/sh: 1: src/main.rs: Permission denied\\n...\", // But contains \"error\" text\n    \"metadata\": {\n      \"exit\": 0 // Exit code confirms success\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### The Fundamental Problem\n\nThe `detectOutputErrors()` function correctly identifies completed tools to skip, but the error patterns are still being matched against the combined output that includes all JSON lines. The issue is in how the filtering interacts with the final pattern matching:\n\n```javascript\n// Line 509-510: Combines filtered stdout with stderr\nconst filteredOutput = nonToolOutputLines.join('\\n') + '\\n' + stderrOutput;\n\n// Line 513-517: Scans the filtered output\nfor (const { pattern, type } of errorPatterns) {\n  const match = filteredOutput.match(pattern);\n  if (match) {\n    return { detected: true, type, match: match[0] };\n  }\n}\n```\n\nThe bug occurs because the JSON lines are being added to `nonToolOutputLines` array even when they should be fully skipped. The tool output JSON line contains the \"Permission denied\" text as a string value, which gets matched.\n\n---\n\n## Evidence from Logs\n\n### Tool Output (lines 1838-1851 in log)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"type\": \"tool_use\",\n  \"part\": {\n    \"type\": \"tool\",\n    \"callID\": \"call_40598996\",\n    \"tool\": \"bash\",\n    \"state\": {\n      \"status\": \"completed\",\n      \"input\": {\n        \"command\": \"gh pr edit 2 ... --body \\\"...`src/main.rs`...\\\"\"\n      },\n      \"output\": \"/bin/sh: 1: src/main.rs: Permission denied\\n...https://...pull/2\\n\",\n      \"metadata\": {\n        \"exit\": 0\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Error Detection Output (lines 2463-2489 in log)\n\n```\n[2025-12-09T07:39:45.395Z] [ERROR]\n\n❌ Agent command failed: PermissionError detected in output despite exit code 0\n[2025-12-09T07:39:45.396Z] [ERROR]    Error pattern matched: Permission denied\n...\n{\n  \"type\": \"error\",\n  \"exitCode\": 0,\n  \"errorDetectedInOutput\": true,\n  \"errorType\": \"PermissionError\",\n  \"errorMatch\": \"Permission denied\"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Implemented Solution: Trust Exit Code\n\n### Key Insight\n\nThe `@link-assistant/agent` package now properly handles errors:\n\n- Returns exit code 1 on errors (not exit code 0)\n- Outputs explicit JSON error messages (`type: \"error\"` or `type: \"step_error\"`)\n\nThis means we can **trust the exit code** and should not scan output for error patterns.\n\n### Why Pattern Matching Was Removed\n\nPattern matching in agent output causes false positives because:\n\n1. AI agents execute bash commands that produce warnings like \"Permission denied\"\n2. AI agents read source code that contains error-related strings\n3. AI agents may encounter and report error messages as part of their normal workflow\n\nAll these scenarios involve error-like text appearing in output but **do not indicate failure**.\n\n### Final Implementation\n\nThe solution was simplified to only detect explicit JSON error messages:\n\n```javascript\n// Simplified error detection for agent tool\n// Issue #886: Trust exit code - agent now properly returns code 1 on errors\nconst detectAgentErrors = stdoutOutput => {\n  const lines = stdoutOutput.split('\\n');\n\n  for (const line of lines) {\n    if (!line.trim()) continue;\n\n    try {\n      const msg = JSON.parse(line);\n\n      // Check for explicit error message types from agent\n      if (msg.type === 'error' || msg.type === 'step_error') {\n        return { detected: true, type: 'AgentError', match: msg.message || line.substring(0, 100) };\n      }\n    } catch {\n      // Not JSON - ignore for error detection\n      continue;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return { detected: false };\n};\n```\n\n### Error Detection Now Based On\n\n1. **Exit code** (non-zero = error) - Primary error signal\n2. **Explicit JSON error messages** (`type: \"error\"` or `type: \"step_error\"`)\n3. **Usage limit detection** (handled separately)\n\n### What Was Removed\n\n- All error pattern matching (permission denied, ENOENT, stack traces, etc.)\n- Complex JSON parsing to filter tool outputs\n- Pattern scanning in stderr\n\n---\n\n## Impact of \"No Logs in Comments\"\n\nThe second part of issue #886 - \"no logs in the comments\" - is a **direct consequence** of the false positive error detection.\n\n### Flow Analysis:\n\n1. `solve.mjs` calls agent with `--attach-logs` flag\n2. Agent completes and returns\n3. `agent.lib.mjs` checks for errors in output\n4. FALSE POSITIVE: Error detected despite exit code 0\n5. Agent execution marked as FAILED\n6. Log attachment code path is skipped (only runs on success)\n7. PR #2 has no logs attached\n\n### Code Path (src/solve.results.lib.mjs):\n\n```javascript\n// Line ~503-514\nif (shouldAttachLogs && getLogFile()) {\n  // Only called on success path, NOT on error path\n}\n```\n\n### Fix Implication:\n\nFixing the false positive error detection will automatically restore the log attachment functionality, as the agent will correctly be marked as successful.\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Summary\n\n### Files Modified\n\n| File                                         | Change                                                                |\n| -------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------- |\n| `src/agent.lib.mjs`                          | Replaced `detectOutputErrors()` with simplified `detectAgentErrors()` |\n| `tests/test-agent-error-detection.mjs`       | Updated tests to match new simplified logic                           |\n| `experiments/test-agent-error-detection.mjs` | Updated experiment to demonstrate fix                                 |\n\n### Test Results\n\nAll 10 test cases pass:\n\n- Issue #886 scenario (bash with shell warnings) - No false positive ✅\n- Issue #873 scenario (source code with error strings) - No false positive ✅\n- Explicit JSON error messages - Detected correctly ✅\n- Clean output - No false detection ✅\n\n---\n\n## Related Issues\n\n- Issue #873: Phantom error detection for `--tool agent` (similar root cause, different trigger)\n- Issue #867: Agent error not treated as error (related to error detection logic)\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThis issue highlighted that pattern matching for error detection in agent output is fundamentally flawed. The previous approach attempted to identify errors by scanning output text for patterns like \"permission denied\", \"ENOENT\", or stack traces. However, this approach causes false positives because:\n\n1. AI agents execute bash commands that may produce warnings\n2. AI agents read/process source code containing error-related text\n3. AI agents report errors they encounter as part of their normal workflow\n\n**The solution**: Trust the exit code. The `@link-assistant/agent` package now properly returns:\n\n- Exit code 1 on actual errors\n- JSON error messages (`type: \"error\"`) for structured error reporting\n\nThis simple approach eliminates false positives while still detecting real failures.\n\n**Artifacts:**\n\n- Full log file: `solve-2025-12-09T07-37-32-414Z.log`\n- Test PR: https://github.com/konard/test-hello-world-019b020a-a43c-7544-aaa1-220021798428/pull/2\n",
      "numLines": 355,
      "startLine": 1,
      "totalLines": 355
    }

When the agent reads source code files containing error-related text (like \"permission denied\" in error handling code), these strings trigger false positive error detection despite successful execution (exit code 0).\n     8→\n     9→**Impact:** Valid agent executions are incorrectly flagged as failures, causing workflow interruptions and reporting false errors to users.\n    10→\n    11→**Fix Status:** Solution identified and documented.\n    12→\n    13→---\n    14→\n    15→## Timeline / Sequence of Events\n    16→\n    17→### Event 1: Agent Execution Starts\n    18→\n    19→- **Time:** 2025-12-09T01:36:28.882Z\n    20→- **Action:** Agent starts working on issue #692\n    21→- **File:** PR #711 context\n    22→- **Status:** Normal execution\n    23→\n    24→### Event 2: Agent Reads Source File\n    25→\n    26→- **Time:** ~2025-12-09T01:37:18Z\n    27→- **Action:** Agent uses \"read\" tool to read `src/solve.auto-pr.lib.mjs`\n    28→- **Log Location:** Line 1290-1301 in full-agent-log.txt\n    29→- **Content:** File contains error handling code with strings like:\n    30→  - 2025-12-09T01:37:53.619Z\n    57→- **Action:** Agent completes with step_finish\n    58→- **Exit Code:** 0 (success)\n    59→- **Log:** Shows successful summary message\n    60→\n    61→### Event 5: \"permission denied\",\n    91→    \"message\": \"Agent command failed: PermissionError detected in output despite exit code 0\",\n    92→    \"sessionId\": null,\n    93→    \"limitReached\": false,\n    94→    \"limitResetTime\": null\n    95→  }\n    96→  ```\n    97→\n    98→---\n    99→\n   100→## Root Cause Analysis\n   101→\n   102→### Primary Cause\n   103→\n   104→The error detection logic in `src/agent.lib.mjs:454-484` uses regex patterns to scan for errors in combined stdout+stderr output. The critical flaw is at **line 471**:\n   105→\n   106→```javascript\n   107→// Check both stdout and stderr for error patterns\n   108→const combinedOutput = fullOutput + allStderr;\n   109→```\n   110→\n   111→This `fullOutput` includes **all JSON-formatted tool outputs** from the agent, including the complete content of files read by the agent. When source code contains error-related strings (as normal error handling code does), these trigger false positives.\n   112→\n   113→### Why This Design Exists\n   114→\n   115→The error detection was implemented to catch cases where:\n   116→\n   117→1. The Node.js process exits with code 0 despite throwing uncaught exceptions\n   118→2. Actual errors are reported in agent output but don't cause non-zero exit codes\n   119→3. Reference: Line 455 comment: \"Agent may exit with code 0 despite throwing errors (Node.js uncaught exception behavior)\"\n   120→\n   121→### The Fundamental Conflict\n   122→\n   123→- **Need:** Detect real errors that don't produce non-zero exit codes\n   124→- **Problem:** Can't distinguish between:\n   125→  - Actual error messages in agent output\n   126→  - Error-related text in source code being read/processed by agent\n   127→  - Error-related text in agent's analysis/summary of code\n   128→\n   129→### Examples of Problematic Patterns (src/agent.lib.mjs:456-468)\n   130→\n   131→```javascript\n   132→const errorPatterns = [\n   133→  { pattern: /ProviderModelNotFoundError/i, type: 'ProviderModelNotFoundError' },\n   134→  { pattern: /ModelNotFoundError/i, type: 'ModelNotFoundError' },\n   135→  { pattern: /\\s+at\\s+\\S+\\s+\\([^)]+:\\d+:\\d+\\)/m, type: 'StackTrace' },\n   136→  { pattern: /throw new \\w+Error/i, type: 'ThrowError' }, // ⚠️ Matches source code\n   137→  { pattern: /authentication failed/i, type: 'AuthenticationError' }, // ⚠️ Matches strings\n   138→  { pattern: /permission denied/i, type: 'PermissionError' }, // ⚠️ THIS ONE!\n   139→  { pattern: /ENOENT|EACCES|EPERM/i, type: 'FileSystemError' },\n   140→  { pattern: /TypeError:|ReferenceError:|SyntaxError:/i, type: 'JavaScriptError' },\n   141→  { pattern: /Cannot read propert(y|ies) of (undefined|null)/i, type: 'NullReferenceError' },\n   142→  { pattern: /Uncaught Exception:/i, type: 'UncaughtException' },\n   143→  { pattern: /Unhandled Rejection/i, type: 'UnhandledRejection' },\n   144→];\n   145→```\n   146→\n   147→**High-risk patterns** (likely to match source code):\n   148→\n   149→- `/permission denied/i` - Common in error handling code\n   150→- `/throw new \\w+Error/i` - Appears in any code with error throwing\n   151→- `/authentication failed/i` - Common in auth-related code\n   152→\n   153→---\n   154→\n   155→## Research Findings: Best Practices for Error Detection (2025)\n   156→\n   157→Based on web research, industry best practices for avoiding false positives in stdout/stderr error detection include:\n   158→\n   159→### 1. **Exit Codes are Primary Source of Truth**\n   160→\n   161→- Logging output is not the primary output of a program\n   162→- Stderr exists specifically to separate core program output from error/logging\n   163→- **Source:** [How to use stdout and stderr](https://julienharbulot.com/python-cli-streams.html)\n   164→\n   165→### 2. **Context-Aware Parsing**\n   166→\n   167→- Pattern matching should validate context, not just presence of text\n   168→- Distinguish between keywords in the right place vs. wrong place\n   169→- **Source:** [Regex Log Parser | Panther Docs](https://docs.panther.com/data-onboarding/custom-log-types/regex-parser)\n   170→\n   171→### 3. **Structured Format Validation**\n   172→\n   173→- Validate that extracted data matches expected structure (e.g., starts with `{` or `[`)\n   174→- Use structured formats over plain text when possible\n   175→- **Source:** [AI Agent structured output parser · Issue #21174](https://github.com/n8n-io/n8n/issues/21174)\n   176→\n   177→### 4. **Stream Separation**\n   178→\n   179→- Separating stderr from stdout allows distinguishing expected output from errors\n   180→- Mixing streams makes debugging harder\n   181→- **Source:** [What Are stdin, stdout, and stderr on Linux?](https://www.howtogeek.com/435903/what-are-stdin-stdout-and-stderr-on-linux/)\n   182→\n   183→### 5. **Multi-layered Validation**\n   184→\n   185→- Combine exit codes, structured formats, and pattern matching\n   186→- Regular testing against diverse log samples\n   187→- **Source:** [How to avoid False Positives in Testing | BrowserStack](https://www.browserstack.com/guide/false-positives-and-false-negatives-in-testing)\n   188→\n   189→---\n   190→\n   191→## Proposed Solutions\n   192→\n   193→### Solution 1: Parse JSON Structure (RECOMMENDED)\n   194→\n   195→**Approach:** Parse agent output as structured JSON and only check specific fields for errors, not tool output content.\n   196→\n   197→**Implementation:**\n   198→\n   199→```javascript\n   200→// Instead of scanning all output, parse JSON messages and check specific fields\n   201→const detectOutputErrors = output => {\n   202→  const lines = output.split('\\n');\n   203→\n   204→  for (const line of lines) {\n   205→    // Skip empty lines\n   206→    if (!line.trim()) continue;\n   207→\n   208→    try {\n   209→      const msg = JSON.parse(line);\n   210→\n   211→      // Only check error-specific message types\n   212→      if (msg.type === 'error' || msg.type === 'step_error') {\n   213→        return { detected: true, type: 'AgentError', match: line };\n   214→      }\n   215→\n   216→      // Check for error state in tool messages\n   217→      if (msg.type === 'tool' && msg.state?.status === 'failed') {\n   218→        return { detected: true, type: 'ToolError', match: msg.state.error };\n   219→      }\n   220→    } catch (e) {\n   221→      // Not JSON or malformed - could be actual error output\n   222→      // Only check non-JSON lines for error patterns\n   223→      for (const { pattern, type } of errorPatterns) {\n   224→        const match = line.match(pattern);\n   225→        if (match) {\n   226→          return { detected: true, type, match: match[0] };\n   227→        }\n   228→      }\n   229→    }\n   230→  }\n   231→\n   232→  return { detected: false };\n   233→};\n   234→```\n   235→\n   236→**Pros:**\n   237→\n   238→- ✅ Eliminates false positives from tool output content\n   239→- ✅ Leverages structured data format\n   240→- ✅ More maintainable and precise\n   241→- ✅ Can still catch non-JSON error output\n   242→\n   243→**Cons:**\n   244→\n   245→- ⚠️ Requires understanding agent's JSON message structure\n   246→- ⚠️ May miss errors if agent changes output format\n   247→\n   248→### Solution 2: Enhanced Pattern Specificity\n   249→\n   250→**Approach:** Make regex patterns more specific to avoid matching common code patterns.\n   251→\n   252→**Implementation:**\n   253→\n   254→```javascript\n   255→const errorPatterns = [\n   256→  { pattern: /ProviderModelNotFoundError/i, type: 'ProviderModelNotFoundError' },\n   257→  { pattern: /ModelNotFoundError/i, type: 'ModelNotFoundError' },\n   258→  { pattern: /\\s+at\\s+\\S+\\s+\\([^)]+:\\d+:\\d+\\)/m, type: 'StackTrace' },\n   259→\n   260→  // More specific patterns with context\n   261→  { pattern: /^Error:.*permission denied/im, type: 'PermissionError' }, // Line must start with \"Error:\"\n   262→  { pattern: /^throw new \\w+Error/im, type: 'ThrowError' }, // Only if at start of line (unlikely in JSON)\n   263→  { pattern: /^.*?authentication failed.*?$/im, type: 'AuthenticationError' },\n   264→\n   265→  { pattern: /ENOENT|EACCES|EPERM/i, type: 'FileSystemError' },\n   266→  { pattern: /TypeError:|ReferenceError:|SyntaxError:/i, type: 'JavaScriptError' },\n   267→  { pattern: /Cannot read propert(y|ies) of (undefined|null)/i, type: 'NullReferenceError' },\n   268→  { pattern: /Uncaught Exception:/i, type: 'UncaughtException' },\n   269→  { pattern: /Unhandled Rejection/i, type: 'UnhandledRejection' },\n   270→];\n   271→```\n   272→\n   273→**Pros:**\n   274→\n   275→- ✅ Smaller code change\n   276→- ✅ Backward compatible\n   277→\n   278→**Cons:**\n   279→\n   280→- ❌ Still prone to false positives\n   281→- ❌ Harder to maintain\n   282→- ❌ Doesn't address fundamental issue\n   283→\n   284→### Solution 3: Exclude Tool Output Content\n   285→\n   286→**Approach:** Filter out JSON tool messages with `type: \"tool\"` before scanning for errors.\n   287→\n   288→**Implementation:**\n   289→\n   290→```javascript\n   291→const detectOutputErrors = output => {\n   292→  // Remove tool output content from error scanning\n   293→  const lines = output.split('\\n');\n   294→  const filteredLines = [];\n   295→\n   296→  for (const line of lines) {\n   297→    if (!line.trim()) continue;\n   298→\n   299→    try {\n   300→      const msg = JSON.parse(line);\n   301→      // Skip tool output but keep error/warning messages\n   302→      if (msg.type === 'tool' && msg.state?.status === 'completed') {\n   303→        continue; // Don't scan successful tool outputs\n   304→      }\n   305→    } catch (e) {\n   306→      // Not JSON, keep for scanning\n   307→    }\n   308→\n   309→    filteredLines.push(line);\n   310→  }\n   311→\n   312→  const filteredOutput = filteredLines.join('\\n');\n   313→\n   314→  // Now scan the filtered output\n   315→  for (const { pattern, type } of errorPatterns) {\n   316→    const match = filteredOutput.match(pattern);\n   317→    if (match) {\n   318→      return { detected: true, type, match: match[0] };\n   319→    }\n   320→  }\n   321→\n   322→  return { detected: false };\n   323→};\n   324→```\n   325→\n   326→**Pros:**\n   327→\n   328→- ✅ Directly addresses the root cause\n   329→- ✅ Simple logic\n   330→- ✅ Maintains existing error patterns\n   331→\n   332→**Cons:**\n   333→\n   334→- ⚠️ Requires parsing every line\n   335→- ⚠️ May miss errors in tool outputs (but that's probably okay)\n   336→\n   337→### Solution 4: Stderr-Only Scanning\n   338→\n   339→**Approach:** Only scan stderr for error patterns, trust stdout is structured data.\n   340→\n   341→**Implementation:**\n   342→\n   343→```javascript\n   344→// Only check stderr for error patterns, not stdout\n   345→const outputError = detectOutputErrors(allStderr); // Remove fullOutput\n   346→```\n   347→\n   348→**Pros:**\n   349→\n   350→- ✅ Simplest change\n   351→- ✅ Aligns with Unix conventions (stderr = errors)\n   352→- ✅ Completely eliminates tool output false positives\n   353→\n   354→**Cons:**\n   355→\n   356→- ❌ May miss errors that only appear in stdout\n   357→- ❌ Depends on agent properly using stderr for errors\n   358→\n   359→---\n   360→\n   361→## Recommendation\n   362→\n   363→**Implement Solution 1 (Parse JSON Structure)** as the primary fix, with **Solution 4 (Stderr-Only)** as a fallback.\n   364→\n   365→### Rationale:\n   366→\n   367→1. **Solution 1** addresses the root cause by understanding the structured nature of agent output\n   368→2. It's the most robust long-term solution\n   369→3. It aligns with 2025 best practices for error detection\n   370→4. **Solution 4** can be used as an additional filter to further reduce false positives\n   371→\n   372→### Implementation Plan:\n   373→\n   374→1. Implement JSON-aware error detection (Solution 1)\n   375→2. Add stderr-priority checking (Solution 4 as supplement)\n   376→3. Keep existing patterns but apply them only to non-JSON lines\n   377→4. Add tests for common false positive scenarios\n   378→5. Monitor for any missed real errors\n   379→\n   380→---\n   381→\n   382→## Testing Strategy\n   383→\n   384→### Test Case 1: Current Bug Scenario\n   385→\n   386→- **Input:** Agent reads file containing \"permission denied\" in source code\n   387→- **Expected:** No error detected (exit code 0, successful execution)\n   388→- **Current Result:** ❌ False positive error\n   389→- **After Fix:** ✅ No error detected\n   390→\n   391→### Test Case 2: Real Permission Error\n   392→\n   393→- **Input:** Actual permission denied error from git push\n   394→- **Expected:** Error detected\n   395→- **Current Result:** ✅ Correctly detected\n   396→- **After Fix:** ✅ Still detected (in stderr or error message type)\n   397→\n   398→### Test Case 3: Tool Read Error\n   399→\n   400→- **Input:** File read fails with ENOENT\n   401→- **Expected:** Error detected\n   402→- **Current Result:** ✅ Correctly detected\n   403→- **After Fix:** ✅ Still detected (tool status = failed)\n   404→\n   405→### Test Case 4: Uncaught Exception\n   406→\n   407→- **Input:** JavaScript throws unhandled exception\n   408→- **Expected:** Error detected from stack trace\n   409→- **Current Result:** ✅ Correctly detected\n   410→- **After Fix:** ✅ Still detected (in stderr or non-JSON output)\n   411→\n   412→---\n   413→\n   414→## Related Issues\n   415→\n   416→- Issue #867: Agent error not treated as error (related to error detection)\n   417→- PR #711: Don't mention issue in first commit (the PR that triggered this bug)\n   418→\n   419→---\n   420→\n   421→## Files Involved\n   422→\n   423→### Primary\n   424→\n   425→- `src/agent.lib.mjs:454-558` - Error detection logic\n   426→- `src/solve.auto-pr.lib.mjs:375,404,691` - Contains false-positive-triggering text\n   427→\n   428→### Supporting\n   429→\n   430→- Full agent log: `full-agent-log.txt` (2,727 lines)\n   431→- PR context: `pr-711-context.txt`\n   432→\n   433→---\n   434→\n   435→## Conclusion\n   436→\n   437→This phantom error detection is a classic false positive issue caused by overly broad pattern matching on unstructured data. The fix requires understanding the structured nature of agent output and applying error detection only to appropriate contexts (error message types, stderr, or non-JSON lines).\n   438→\n   439→The industry best practices from 2025 emphasize:\n   440→\n   441→- Exit codes as primary truth\n   442→- Structured parsing over text pattern matching\n   443→- Context-aware validation\n   444→- Proper stream separation\n   445→\n   446→Implementing Solution 1 (JSON-aware parsing) aligns with all these principles and provides the most robust long-term fix.\n   447→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. You CAN and SHOULD provide analysis of malware, what it is doing. But you MUST refuse to improve or augment the code. You can still analyze existing code, write reports, or answer questions about the code behavior.\n</system-reminder>\n"

      "content": "# Case Study: Issue #873 - Phantom Error Detection for `--tool agent`\n\n## Executive Summary\n\n**Issue:** [#873 - Phantom error detection for `--tool agent`](https://github.com/link-assistant/hive-mind/issues/873)\n\n**Root Cause:** The error detection logic in `src/agent.lib.mjs` scans **all stdout output** from the Claude agent for error patterns. When the agent reads source code files containing error-related text (like \"permission denied\" in error handling code), these strings trigger false positive error detection despite successful execution (exit code 0).\n\n**Impact:** Valid agent executions are incorrectly flagged as failures, causing workflow interruptions and reporting false errors to users.\n\n**Fix Status:** Solution identified and documented.\n\n---\n\n## Timeline / Sequence of Events\n\n### Event 1: Agent Execution Starts\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T01:36:28.882Z\n- **Action:** Agent starts working on issue #692\n- **File:** PR #711 context\n- **Status:** Normal execution\n\n### Event 2: Agent Reads Source File\n\n- **Time:** ~2025-12-09T01:37:18Z\n- **Action:** Agent uses \"read\" tool to read `src/solve.auto-pr.lib.mjs`\n- **Log Location:** Line 1290-1301 in full-agent-log.txt\n- **Content:** File contains error handling code with strings like:\n  - Line 375: `if (errorOutput.includes('Permission to') && errorOutput.includes('denied'))`\n  - Line 404: `await log(\\`\\\\n\\${formatAligned('❌', 'PERMISSION DENIED:', 'Cannot push to repository')}\\`, { level: 'error' });`\n  - Line 691: `// User doesn't have permission, but that's okay - we just won't assign`\n\n### Event 3: Agent Tool Output Captured\n\n- **Time:** During execution\n- **Action:** The entire file content is part of the JSON tool output and sent to stdout\n- **Data Structure:**\n  ```json\n  {\n    \"type\": \"tool\",\n    \"callID\": \"call_48792570\",\n    \"tool\": \"read\",\n    \"state\": {\n      \"status\": \"completed\",\n      \"input\": {\n        \"filePath\": \"src/solve.auto-pr.lib.mjs\"\n      },\n      \"output\": \"<file>\\n00001| /**\\n... [entire file content including error handling code] ...\"\n    }\n  }\n  ```\n\n### Event 4: Agent Completes Successfully\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T01:37:53.619Z\n- **Action:** Agent completes with step_finish\n- **Exit Code:** 0 (success)\n- **Log:** Shows successful summary message\n\n### Event 5: Error Detection Runs (BUG TRIGGERED)\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T01:37:53.673Z\n- **Location:** `src/agent.lib.mjs:454-484`\n- **Action:** Error detection scans `combinedOutput = fullOutput + allStderr`\n- **Pattern Matched:** `/permission denied/i` at line 462\n- **Match Found:** \"permission denied\" text from source code in tool output\n- **Result:** False positive error detected\n\n### Event 6: Error Reported\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T01:37:53.673Z\n- **Log Output:**\n  ```\n  ❌ Agent command failed: PermissionError detected in output despite exit code 0\n     Error pattern matched: permission denied\n     Last output context (truncated): ... solution reduces timeline noise ...\n  ```\n\n### Event 7: Structured Error JSON Logged\n\n- **Time:** 2025-12-09T01:37:53.674Z\n- **Error Details:**\n  ```json\n  {\n    \"type\": \"error\",\n    \"exitCode\": 0,\n    \"errorDetectedInOutput\": true,\n    \"errorType\": \"PermissionError\",\n    \"errorMatch\": \"permission denied\",\n    \"message\": \"Agent command failed: PermissionError detected in output despite exit code 0\",\n    \"sessionId\": null,\n    \"limitReached\": false,\n    \"limitResetTime\": null\n  }\n  ```\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause Analysis\n\n### Primary Cause\n\nThe error detection logic in `src/agent.lib.mjs:454-484` uses regex patterns to scan for errors in combined stdout+stderr output. The critical flaw is at **line 471**:\n\n```javascript\n// Check both stdout and stderr for error patterns\nconst combinedOutput = fullOutput + allStderr;\n```\n\nThis `fullOutput` includes **all JSON-formatted tool outputs** from the agent, including the complete content of files read by the agent. When source code contains error-related strings (as normal error handling code does), these trigger false positives.\n\n### Why This Design Exists\n\nThe error detection was implemented to catch cases where:\n\n1. The Node.js process exits with code 0 despite throwing uncaught exceptions\n2. Actual errors are reported in agent output but don't cause non-zero exit codes\n3. Reference: Line 455 comment: \"Agent may exit with code 0 despite throwing errors (Node.js uncaught exception behavior)\"\n\n### The Fundamental Conflict\n\n- **Need:** Detect real errors that don't produce non-zero exit codes\n- **Problem:** Can't distinguish between:\n  - Actual error messages in agent output\n  - Error-related text in source code being read/processed by agent\n  - Error-related text in agent's analysis/summary of code\n\n### Examples of Problematic Patterns (src/agent.lib.mjs:456-468)\n\n```javascript\nconst errorPatterns = [\n  { pattern: /ProviderModelNotFoundError/i, type: 'ProviderModelNotFoundError' },\n  { pattern: /ModelNotFoundError/i, type: 'ModelNotFoundError' },\n  { pattern: /\\s+at\\s+\\S+\\s+\\([^)]+:\\d+:\\d+\\)/m, type: 'StackTrace' },\n  { pattern: /throw new \\w+Error/i, type: 'ThrowError' }, // ⚠️ Matches source code\n  { pattern: /authentication failed/i, type: 'AuthenticationError' }, // ⚠️ Matches strings\n  { pattern: /permission denied/i, type: 'PermissionError' }, // ⚠️ THIS ONE!\n  { pattern: /ENOENT|EACCES|EPERM/i, type: 'FileSystemError' },\n  { pattern: /TypeError:|ReferenceError:|SyntaxError:/i, type: 'JavaScriptError' },\n  { pattern: /Cannot read propert(y|ies) of (undefined|null)/i, type: 'NullReferenceError' },\n  { pattern: /Uncaught Exception:/i, type: 'UncaughtException' },\n  { pattern: /Unhandled Rejection/i, type: 'UnhandledRejection' },\n];\n```\n\n**High-risk patterns** (likely to match source code):\n\n- `/permission denied/i` - Common in error handling code\n- `/throw new \\w+Error/i` - Appears in any code with error throwing\n- `/authentication failed/i` - Common in auth-related code\n\n---\n\n## Research Findings: Best Practices for Error Detection (2025)\n\nBased on web research, industry best practices for avoiding false positives in stdout/stderr error detection include:\n\n### 1. **Exit Codes are Primary Source of Truth**\n\n- Logging output is not the primary output of a program\n- Stderr exists specifically to separate core program output from error/logging\n- **Source:** [How to use stdout and stderr](https://julienharbulot.com/python-cli-streams.html)\n\n### 2. **Context-Aware Parsing**\n\n- Pattern matching should validate context, not just presence of text\n- Distinguish between keywords in the right place vs. wrong place\n- **Source:** [Regex Log Parser | Panther Docs](https://docs.panther.com/data-onboarding/custom-log-types/regex-parser)\n\n### 3. **Structured Format Validation**\n\n- Validate that extracted data matches expected structure (e.g., starts with `{` or `[`)\n- Use structured formats over plain text when possible\n- **Source:** [AI Agent structured output parser · Issue #21174](https://github.com/n8n-io/n8n/issues/21174)\n\n### 4. **Stream Separation**\n\n- Separating stderr from stdout allows distinguishing expected output from errors\n- Mixing streams makes debugging harder\n- **Source:** [What Are stdin, stdout, and stderr on Linux?](https://www.howtogeek.com/435903/what-are-stdin-stdout-and-stderr-on-linux/)\n\n### 5. **Multi-layered Validation**\n\n- Combine exit codes, structured formats, and pattern matching\n- Regular testing against diverse log samples\n- **Source:** [How to avoid False Positives in Testing | BrowserStack](https://www.browserstack.com/guide/false-positives-and-false-negatives-in-testing)\n\n---\n\n## Proposed Solutions\n\n### Solution 1: Parse JSON Structure (RECOMMENDED)\n\n**Approach:** Parse agent output as structured JSON and only check specific fields for errors, not tool output content.\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// Instead of scanning all output, parse JSON messages and check specific fields\nconst detectOutputErrors = output => {\n  const lines = output.split('\\n');\n\n  for (const line of lines) {\n    // Skip empty lines\n    if (!line.trim()) continue;\n\n    try {\n      const msg = JSON.parse(line);\n\n      // Only check error-specific message types\n      if (msg.type === 'error' || msg.type === 'step_error') {\n        return { detected: true, type: 'AgentError', match: line };\n      }\n\n      // Check for error state in tool messages\n      if (msg.type === 'tool' && msg.state?.status === 'failed') {\n        return { detected: true, type: 'ToolError', match: msg.state.error };\n      }\n    } catch (e) {\n      // Not JSON or malformed - could be actual error output\n      // Only check non-JSON lines for error patterns\n      for (const { pattern, type } of errorPatterns) {\n        const match = line.match(pattern);\n        if (match) {\n          return { detected: true, type, match: match[0] };\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  return { detected: false };\n};\n```\n\n**Pros:**\n\n- ✅ Eliminates false positives from tool output content\n- ✅ Leverages structured data format\n- ✅ More maintainable and precise\n- ✅ Can still catch non-JSON error output\n\n**Cons:**\n\n- ⚠️ Requires understanding agent's JSON message structure\n- ⚠️ May miss errors if agent changes output format\n\n### Solution 2: Enhanced Pattern Specificity\n\n**Approach:** Make regex patterns more specific to avoid matching common code patterns.\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\nconst errorPatterns = [\n  { pattern: /ProviderModelNotFoundError/i, type: 'ProviderModelNotFoundError' },\n  { pattern: /ModelNotFoundError/i, type: 'ModelNotFoundError' },\n  { pattern: /\\s+at\\s+\\S+\\s+\\([^)]+:\\d+:\\d+\\)/m, type: 'StackTrace' },\n\n  // More specific patterns with context\n  { pattern: /^Error:.*permission denied/im, type: 'PermissionError' }, // Line must start with \"Error:\"\n  { pattern: /^throw new \\w+Error/im, type: 'ThrowError' }, // Only if at start of line (unlikely in JSON)\n  { pattern: /^.*?authentication failed.*?$/im, type: 'AuthenticationError' },\n\n  { pattern: /ENOENT|EACCES|EPERM/i, type: 'FileSystemError' },\n  { pattern: /TypeError:|ReferenceError:|SyntaxError:/i, type: 'JavaScriptError' },\n  { pattern: /Cannot read propert(y|ies) of (undefined|null)/i, type: 'NullReferenceError' },\n  { pattern: /Uncaught Exception:/i, type: 'UncaughtException' },\n  { pattern: /Unhandled Rejection/i, type: 'UnhandledRejection' },\n];\n```\n\n**Pros:**\n\n- ✅ Smaller code change\n- ✅ Backward compatible\n\n**Cons:**\n\n- ❌ Still prone to false positives\n- ❌ Harder to maintain\n- ❌ Doesn't address fundamental issue\n\n### Solution 3: Exclude Tool Output Content\n\n**Approach:** Filter out JSON tool messages with `type: \"tool\"` before scanning for errors.\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\nconst detectOutputErrors = output => {\n  // Remove tool output content from error scanning\n  const lines = output.split('\\n');\n  const filteredLines = [];\n\n  for (const line of lines) {\n    if (!line.trim()) continue;\n\n    try {\n      const msg = JSON.parse(line);\n      // Skip tool output but keep error/warning messages\n      if (msg.type === 'tool' && msg.state?.status === 'completed') {\n        continue; // Don't scan successful tool outputs\n      }\n    } catch (e) {\n      // Not JSON, keep for scanning\n    }\n\n    filteredLines.push(line);\n  }\n\n  const filteredOutput = filteredLines.join('\\n');\n\n  // Now scan the filtered output\n  for (const { pattern, type } of errorPatterns) {\n    const match = filteredOutput.match(pattern);\n    if (match) {\n      return { detected: true, type, match: match[0] };\n    }\n  }\n\n  return { detected: false };\n};\n```\n\n**Pros:**\n\n- ✅ Directly addresses the root cause\n- ✅ Simple logic\n- ✅ Maintains existing error patterns\n\n**Cons:**\n\n- ⚠️ Requires parsing every line\n- ⚠️ May miss errors in tool outputs (but that's probably okay)\n\n### Solution 4: Stderr-Only Scanning\n\n**Approach:** Only scan stderr for error patterns, trust stdout is structured data.\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// Only check stderr for error patterns, not stdout\nconst outputError = detectOutputErrors(allStderr); // Remove fullOutput\n```\n\n**Pros:**\n\n- ✅ Simplest change\n- ✅ Aligns with Unix conventions (stderr = errors)\n- ✅ Completely eliminates tool output false positives\n\n**Cons:**\n\n- ❌ May miss errors that only appear in stdout\n- ❌ Depends on agent properly using stderr for errors\n\n---\n\n## Recommendation\n\n**Implement Solution 1 (Parse JSON Structure)** as the primary fix, with **Solution 4 (Stderr-Only)** as a fallback.\n\n### Rationale:\n\n1. **Solution 1** addresses the root cause by understanding the structured nature of agent output\n2. It's the most robust long-term solution\n3. It aligns with 2025 best practices for error detection\n4. **Solution 4** can be used as an additional filter to further reduce false positives\n\n### Implementation Plan:\n\n1. Implement JSON-aware error detection (Solution 1)\n2. Add stderr-priority checking (Solution 4 as supplement)\n3. Keep existing patterns but apply them only to non-JSON lines\n4. Add tests for common false positive scenarios\n5. Monitor for any missed real errors\n\n---\n\n## Testing Strategy\n\n### Test Case 1: Current Bug Scenario\n\n- **Input:** Agent reads file containing \"permission denied\" in source code\n- **Expected:** No error detected (exit code 0, successful execution)\n- **Current Result:** ❌ False positive error\n- **After Fix:** ✅ No error detected\n\n### Test Case 2: Real Permission Error\n\n- **Input:** Actual permission denied error from git push\n- **Expected:** Error detected\n- **Current Result:** ✅ Correctly detected\n- **After Fix:** ✅ Still detected (in stderr or error message type)\n\n### Test Case 3: Tool Read Error\n\n- **Input:** File read fails with ENOENT\n- **Expected:** Error detected\n- **Current Result:** ✅ Correctly detected\n- **After Fix:** ✅ Still detected (tool status = failed)\n\n### Test Case 4: Uncaught Exception\n\n- **Input:** JavaScript throws unhandled exception\n- **Expected:** Error detected from stack trace\n- **Current Result:** ✅ Correctly detected\n- **After Fix:** ✅ Still detected (in stderr or non-JSON output)\n\n---\n\n## Related Issues\n\n- Issue #867: Agent error not treated as error (related to error detection)\n- PR #711: Don't mention issue in first commit (the PR that triggered this bug)\n\n---\n\n## Files Involved\n\n### Primary\n\n- `src/agent.lib.mjs:454-558` - Error detection logic\n- `src/solve.auto-pr.lib.mjs:375,404,691` - Contains false-positive-triggering text\n\n### Supporting\n\n- Full agent log: `full-agent-log.txt` (2,727 lines)\n- PR context: `pr-711-context.txt`\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThis phantom error detection is a classic false positive issue caused by overly broad pattern matching on unstructured data. The fix requires understanding the structured nature of agent output and applying error detection only to appropriate contexts (error message types, stderr, or non-JSON lines).\n\nThe industry best practices from 2025 emphasize:\n\n- Exit codes as primary truth\n- Structured parsing over text pattern matching\n- Context-aware validation\n- Proper stream separation\n\nImplementing Solution 1 (JSON-aware parsing) aligns with all these principles and provides the most robust long-term fix.\n",

estimate\n   181→    const { baseModelName, isFreeVariant } = getBaseModelForPricing(modelName);\n   182→    let baseModelInfo = null;\n   183→    let pricingCost = modelInfo?.cost;\n   184→\n   185→ model for public pricing\n   187→      baseModelInfo = await fetchModelInfo(baseModelName);\n   188→      if (baseModelInfo && baseModelInfo.cost) {\n   189→        // Use base model pricing for public estimate\n   190→        pricingCost = baseModelInfo.cost;\n   191→        // Update original provider from base model if available\n   192→        if (baseModelInfo.provider && !originalProvider) {\n   193→          originalProvider = baseModelInfo.provider;\n   194→        }\n   195→      }\n   196→    }\n   197→\n   198→    if (modelInfo || baseModelInfo) {\n   199→      const effectiveModelInfo = modelInfo || baseModelInfo;\n   200→      const cost = pricingCost || { input: 0, output: 0, cache_read: 0, cache_write: 0, reasoning: 0 };\n   201→\n   202→      // Calculate public pricing estimate based on original provider prices\n   203→      // Prices are per 1M tokens, so divide by 1,000,000\n   204→      // All priced components from models.dev: input, output, cache_read, cache_write, reasoning\n   205→      const inputCost = (tokenUsage.inputTokens * (cost.input || 0)) / 1_000_000;\n   206→      const outputCost = (tokenUsage.outputTokens * (cost.output || 0)) / 1_000_000;\n   207→      const cacheReadCost = (tokenUsage.cacheReadTokens * (cost.cache_read || 0)) / 1_000_000;\n   208→      const cacheWriteCost = (tokenUsage.cacheWriteTokens * (cost.cache_write || 0)) / 1_000_000;\n   209→      const reasoningCost = (tokenUsage.reasoningTokens * (cost.reasoning || 0)) / 1_000_000;\n   210→\n   211→      const totalCost = inputCost + outputCost + cacheReadCost + cacheWriteCost + reasoningCost;\n   212→\n   213→      // Determine if this is a free model from OpenCode Zen\n   214→      // Models accessed via OpenCode Zen are free, regardless of original provider pricing\n   215→      const isOpencodeFreeModel = providerFromModel === 'opencode' || isFreeVariant || modelName.toLowerCase().includes('free') || modelName.toLowerCase().includes('grok') || providerFromModel === 'moonshot' || providerFromModel === 'openai' || providerFromModel === 'anthropic';\n   216→\n   217→      // Use base model's provider for original provider reference if available\n   218→      const effectiveOriginalProvider = baseModelInfo?.provider || originalProvider || effectiveModelInfo?.provider || null;\n   219→\n   220→      return {\n   221→        modelId,\n   222→        modelName: effectiveModelInfo?.name || modelName,\n   223→        // Issue #1250: Always show OpenCode Zen as actual provider\n   224→        provider: 'OpenCode Zen',\n   225→        // Store original provider for reference in pricing display\n   226→        originalProvider: effectiveOriginalProvider,\n   227→        pricing: {\n   228→          inputPerMillion: cost.input || 0,\n   229→          outputPerMillion: cost.output || 0,\n   230→          cacheReadPerMillion: cost.cache_read || 0,\n   231→          cacheWritePerMillion: cost.cache_write || 0,\n   232→          reasoningPerMillion: cost.reasoning || 0,\n   233→        },\n   234→        tokenUsage,\n   235→        breakdown: {\n   236→          input: inputCost,\n   237→          output: outputCost,\n   238→          cacheRead: cacheReadCost,\n   239→          cacheWrite: cacheWriteCost,\n   240→          reasoning: reasoningCost,\n   241→        },\n   242→        // Public pricing estimate based on original/base model prices\n   243→        totalCostUSD: totalCost,\n   244→        // Actual cost from OpenCode Zen (free for supported models)\n   245→        opencodeCost: isOpencodeFreeModel ? 0 : totalCost,\n   246→        // Keep for backward compatibility - indicates if the accessed model has zero pricing\n   247→        isFreeModel: modelInfo?.cost?.input === 0 && modelInfo?.cost?.output === 0,\n   248→        // New flag to indicate if OpenCode Zen provides this model for free\n   249→        isOpencodeFreeModel,\n   250→        // Issue #1250: Include base model info for transparency\n   251→        baseModelName: baseModelName !== modelName ? baseModelName : null,\n   252→      };\n   253→    }\n   254→    // Model not found in API, return what we have\n   255→    return {\n   256→      modelId,\n   257→      modelName,\n   258→      provider: 'OpenCode Zen',\n   259→      originalProvider,\n   260→      tokenUsage,\n   261→      totalCostUSD: null,\n   262→      opencodeCost: 0, // OpenCode Zen is free\n   263→      isOpencodeFreeModel: true,\n   264→      error: 'Model not found in models.dev API',\n   265→    };\n   266→  } catch (error) {\n   267→    // Error fetching pricing, return with error info\n   268→    return {\n   269→      modelId,\n   270→      modelName,\n   271→      provider: 'OpenCode Zen',\n   272→      originalProvider,\n   273→      tokenUsage,\n   274→      totalCostUSD: null,\n   275→      opencodeCost: 0, // OpenCode Zen is free\n   276→      isOpencodeFreeModel: true,\n   277→      error: error.message,\n   278→    };\n   279→  }\n   280→};\n   281→\n   282→// Model mapping to translate aliases to full model IDs for Agent\n   283→// Agent uses OpenCode Zen's JSON interface and models\n   284→// Issue #1185: Free models use opencode/ prefix (not openai/)\n   285→export const mapModelToId = model => {\n   286→  const modelMap = {\n   287→    grok: 'opencode/grok-code',\n   288→    'grok-code': 'opencode/grok-code',\n   289→    'grok-code-fast-1': 'opencode/grok-code',\n   290→    'big-pickle': 'opencode/big-pickle',\n   291→    'gpt-5-nano': 'opencode/gpt-5-nano',\n   292→    sonnet: 'anthropic/claude-3-5-sonnet',\n   293→    haiku: 'anthropic/claude-3-5-haiku',\n   294→    opus: 'anthropic/claude-3-opus',\n   295→    'gemini-3-pro': 'google/gemini-3-pro',\n   296→    // Free models mapping for issue #1250\n   297→    'kimi-k2.5-free': 'moonshot/kimi-k2.5-free',\n   298→    'gpt-4o-mini': 'openai/gpt-4o-mini',\n   299→    'gpt-4o': 'openai/gpt-4o',\n   300→    'claude-3.5-haiku': 'anthropic/claude-3.5-haiku',\n   301→    'claude-3.5-sonnet': 'anthropic/claude-3.5-sonnet',\n   302→  };\n   303→\n   304→  // Return mapped model ID if it's an alias, otherwise return as-is\n   305→  return modelMap[model] || model;\n   306→};\n   307→\n   308→// Function to validate Agent connection\n   309→export const validateAgentConnection = async (model = 'grok-code-fast-1') => {\n   310→  // Map model alias to full ID\n   311→  const mappedModel = mapModelToId(model);\n   312→\n   313→  // Retry configuration\n   314→  const maxRetries = 3;\n   315→  let retryCount = 0;\n   316→\n   317→  const attemptValidation = async () => {\n   318→    try {\n   319→      if (retryCount === 0) {\n   320→        await log('🔍 Validating Agent connection...');\n   321→      } else {\n   322→        await log(`🔄 Retry attempt ${retryCount}/${maxRetries} for Agent validation...`);\n   323→      }\n   324→\n   325→      // Check if Agent CLI is installed and get version\n   326→      try {\n   327→        const versionResult = await $`timeout ${Math.floor(timeouts.opencodeCli / 1000)} agent --version`;\n   328→        if (versionResult.code === 0) {\n   329→          const version = versionResult.stdout?.toString().trim();\n   330→          if (retryCount === 0) {\n   331→            await log(`📦 Agent CLI failed (${versionError.code}), proceeding with connection test...`);\n   337→        }\n   338→      }\n   339→\n   340→      // Test basic Agent functionality with a simple \"hi\" message\n   341→      // Agent uses the same JSON interface as OpenCode\n   342→      const testResult = await $`printf \"hi\" | timeout ${Math.floor(timeouts.opencodeCli / 1000)} agent --model ${mappedModel}`;\n   343→\n   344→      if (testResult.code !== 0) {\n   345→        const stderr = testResult.stderr?.toString() || '';\n   346→\n   347→        if (stderr.includes('auth') || stderr.includes('login')) For premium models, you may need: opencode auth', {\n   350→            level: 'error',\n   351→          });\n   352→          return false;\n   353→        }\n   354→\n   355→        await log(`❌ Agent validation failed with exit code ${testResult.code}`, { level: 'error' });\n   356→        if (stderr) await log(`   Error: ${stderr.trim()}`, { level: 'error' });\n   357→        return false;\n   358→      }\n   359→\n   360→      // Success\n   361→      await log('✅ Agent connection validated successfully');\n   362→      return true;\n   363→    } catch (error) {\n   364→      await log(`❌ Failed to validate Agent connection: ${error.message}`, { level: 'error' });\n   365→      await log('   💡 Make sure @link-assistant/agent is installed globally: bun install -g @link-assistant/agent', {\n   366→        level: 'error',\n   367→      });\n   368→      return false;\n   369→    }\n   370→  };\n   371→\n   372→  // Start the validation\n   373→  return await attemptValidation();\n   374→};\n   375→\n   376→// Function to handle Agent runtime switching (if applicable)\n   377→export const handleAgentRuntimeSwitch = async () => {\n   378→  // Agent is run not required for this operation');\n   381→};\n   382→\n   383→// Main function to execute Agent with prompts and settings\n   384→export const executeAgent = async params => {\n   385→  const { ${systemPrompt.length}`, { verbose: true });\n   436→    if (feedbackLines && feedbackLines.length > 0) {\n   437→      await log('   Feedback info: Included', { verbose: true });\n   438→    }\n 450→  }\n   451→\n   452→  // Execute the Agent command\n   453→  return await executeAgentCommand({\n   454→    tempDir,\n   455→    branchName,\n   456→    prompt,\n   457→    systemPrompt,\n   458→    argv,\n   459→    log,\n   460→    formatAligned,\n   461→    getResourceSnapshot,\n   462→    forkedRepo,\n   463→    feedbackLines,\n   464→    agentPath,\n   465→    $,\n   466→  });\n   467→};\n   468→\n   469→export const executeAgentCommand = async params => {\n   470→  const { tempDir, branchName, prompt, systemPrompt, argv, log, formatAligned, getResourceSnapshot, forkedRepo, feedbackLines, agentPath, $ } = params;\n   471→\n   472→  // Retry configuration\n   473→  const maxRetries = 3;\n   474→  let retryCount = 0;\n   475→\n   476→  const executeWithRetry = async () => {\n   477→    // Execute agent command from the cloned repository directory\n   478→    if (retryCount === 0) {\n   479→      await log(`\\n${formatAligned('🤖', 'Executing Agent:', argv.model.toUpperCase())}`);\n   480→    } else {\n   481→      await log(`\\n${formatAligned('🔄', 'Retry attempt:', `${retryCount}/${maxRetries}`)}`);\n   482→    }\n   483→\n   484→    if (argv.verbose) {\n   485→      await log(`   Model: ${argv.model}`, { verbose: true });\n   486→      await log(`   Working directory: ${tempDir}`, { verbose: true });\n   487→      await log(`   Branch: ${branchName}`, { verbose: true });\n   488→      await log(`   Prompt length: ${prompt.length} chars`, { verbose: true });\n   489→      await log(`   System prompt length: Memory: ${resourcesBefore.memory.split('\\n')[1]}`, { verbose: true });\n   501→    await log(`   Load: ${resourcesBefore.load}`, { verbose: true });\n   502→\n   503→    // Build Agent command\n   504→    let execCommand;\n   505→\n   506→    // Map model alias to full ID\n   507→    const mappedModel = mapModelToId(argv.model);\n   508→\n   509→    // Build agent command arguments\n   510→    let agentArgs = `--model ${mappedModel}`;\n   511→\n   512→    // Propagate verbose flag to agent for detailed debugging output\n   513→    if (argv.verbose) {\n   514→      agentArgs += ' --verbose';\n   515→    }\n   516→\n   517→    // Agent supports stdin in both plain text and JSON format\n   518→    // We'll combine system and user prompts into a single message\n   519→    const repository workspace to avoid polluting the repo\n   523→    const promptFile = path.join(os.tmpdir(), `agent_prompt_${Date.now()}_${process.pid}.txt`);\n   524→    await fs.writeFile(promptFile, combinedPrompt);\n   525→\n   526→    // Build the full command - pipe the prompt file to agent\n   527→    const fullCommand = `(cd \"${tempDir}\" && cat \"${promptFile}\" | ${agentPath} ${agentArgs})`;\n   528→\n   529→    await log(`\\n${formatAligned('📝', 'Raw command:', '')}`);\n   530→    await log(`${fullCommand}`);\n   531→    await log('');\n   532→\n   533→    try {\n   534→      // Pipe the prompt file to agent via stdin\n   535→      // Use agentArgs which includes --model and optionally --verbose\n   536→      execCommand = $({\n   537→        cwd: tempDir,\n   538→        mirror: false,\n   539→      })`cat ${promptFile} | ${agentPath} ${agentArgs}`;\n   540→\n   541→      await log(`${formatAligned('📋', 'Command details:', '')}`);\n   542→      await ${argv.model.toUpperCase()}`, 2));\n   545→      if (argv.fork && forkedRepo) {\n   546→        await log(formatAligned('🍴', 'Fork:', forkedRepo, 2));\n   547→      }\n   548→\n   549→      await log(`\\n${formatAligned('▶️', 'Streaming output:', '')}\\n`);\n   550→\n   551→      let exitCode = 0;\n   552→      let sessionId = null;\n   553→      let limitReached = false;\n   554→      let limitResetTime = null;\n   555→      let lastMessage = '';\n   556→      let lastTextContent = ''; // Issue #1263: Track last text content for result summary\n   557→      let fullOutput = ''; // Collect all output for error detection (kept for backward compatibility)\n   558→      // Issue #1201: Track error events detected during streaming for reliable error detection\n   559→      // Post-hoc detection on fullOutput can miss errors if NDJSON lines get concatenated without newlines\n   560→      let streamingErrorDetected = false;\n   561→      let streamingErrorMessage = null;\n   562→      // Issue #1276: Track successful completion events to clear error flags\n   563→      // When agent emits session.idle or disposal events, it means it recovered and completed successfully\n   564→      let agentCompletedSuccessfully = false;\n   565→      // Issue #1250: Accumulate token usage during streaming instead of parsing fullOutput later\n   566→      // This fixes the issue where NDJSON lines get concatenated without newlines, breaking JSON.parse\n   567→      const streamingTokenUsage = {\n   568→        inputTokens: 0,\n   569→        outputTokens: 0,\n   570→        reasoningTokens: 0,\n   571→        cacheReadTokens: 0,\n   572→        cacheWriteTokens: 0,\n   573→        totalCost: 0,\n   574→        stepCount: 0,\n   575→      };\n   576→      // Helper to accumulate tokens from step_finish events during streaming\n   577→      const accumulateTokenUsage = data => {\n   578→        if (data.type === 'step_finish' && data.part?.tokens) {\n   579→          const tokens = data.part.tokens;\n   580→          streamingTokenUsage.stepCount++;\n   581→          if (tokens.input) streamingTokenUsage.inputTokens += tokens.input;\n   582→          if (tokens.output) streamingTokenUsage.outputTokens += tokens.output;\n   583→          if (tokens.reasoning) streamingTokenUsage.reasoningTokens += tokens.reasoning;\n   584→          if (tokens.cache) {\n   585→            if (tokens.cache.read) streamingTokenUsage.cacheReadTokens += tokens.cache.read;\n   586→            if (tokens.cache.write) streamingTokenUsage.cacheWriteTokens += tokens.cache.write;\n   587→          }\n   588→          if (data.part.cost !== undefined) {\n   589→            streamingTokenUsage.totalCost += data.part.cost;\n   590→          }\n   591→        }\n   592→      };\n   593→\n   594→      for await (const chunk of execCommand.stream()) {\n   595→        if (chunk.type === 'stdout') {\n   596→          const output = chunk.data.toString();\n   597→          // Split output into individual lines for NDJSON parsing\n   598→          // Agent outputs NDJSON (newline-delimited JSON) format where each line is a separate JSON object\n   599→          // This allows us to parse each event independently and extract structured data like session IDs\n   600→          const lines = output.split('\\n');\n   601→          for (const line of lines) {\n   602→            if (!line.trim()) continue;\n   603→            try {\n   604→              const data = JSON.parse(line);\n   605→              // Output formatted JSON\n   606→              await log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));\n   607→              // Capture session ID from the first message\n   608→              if (!sessionId && data.sessionID) {\n   609→                sessionId = data.sessionID;\n   610→                await log(`📌 Session ID: ${sessionId}`);\n   611→              }\n   612→              // Issue #1250: Accumulate token usage during streaming\n   613→              accumulateTokenUsage(data);\n   614→              // Issue #1201: Detect error events during streaming for reliable detection\n   615→              if (data.type === 'error' || data.type === 'step_error') {\n   616→                streamingErrorDetected = true;\n   617→                streamingErrorMessage = data.message || data.error || line.substring(0, 100);\n   618→                await log(`⚠️  Error event detected in stream: ${streamingErrorMessage}`, { level: 'warning' });\n   619→              }\n   620→              // Issue #1263: Track text content for result summary\n   621→              // Agent outputs text via 'text', 'assistant', or 'message' type events\n   622→              if (data.type === 'text' && data.text) {\n   623→                lastTextContent = data.text;\n   624→              } else if (data.type === 'assistant' && data.message?.content) {\n   625→                // Extract text from assistant message content\n   626→                const content = Array.isArray(data.message.content) ? data.message.content : [data.message.content];\n   627→                for (const item of content) {\n   628→                  if (item.type === 'text' && item.text) {\n   629→                    lastTextContent = item.text;\n   630→                  }\n   631→                }\n   632→              } else if (data.type === 'message' && data.content) {\n   633→                // Direct message content\n   634→                if (typeof data.content === 'string') {\n   635→                  lastTextContent = data.content;\n   636→                } else if (Array.isArray(data.content)) {\n   637→                  for (const item of data.content) {\n   638→                    if (item.type === 'text' && item.text) {\n   639→                      lastTextContent = item.text;\n   640→                    }\n   641→                  }\n   642→                }\n   643→              } else if (data.type === 'result' && data.result) {\n   644→                // Explicit result message (like Claude outputs)\n   645→                lastTextContent = data.result;\n   646→              }\n   647→              // Issue #1276: Detect successful completion events\n   648→              // When agent emits session.idle or log with \"exiting loop\" message, it completed successfully\n   649→              // This means any previous error events were recovered from (e.g., timeout then retry)\n   650→              if (data.type === 'session.idle' || (data.type === 'log' && data.message === 'exiting loop')) {\n   651→                agentCompletedSuccessfully = true;\n   652→              }\n   653→            } catch {\n   654→              // Not JSON - log as plain text\n   655→              await log(line);\n   656→            }\n   657→          }\n   658→          lastMessage = output;\n   659→          fullOutput += output; // Collect for both pricing calculation and error detection\n   660→        }\n   661→\n   662→        if (chunk.type === 'stderr') {\n   663→          const errorOutput = chunk.data.toString();\n   664→          if (errorOutput) {\n   665→            // Agent sends all output (including verbose logs and structured events) to stderr\n   666→            // Process each line as NDJSON, same as stdout handling\n   667→            const stderrLines = errorOutput.split('\\n');\n   668→            for (const stderrLine of stderrLines) {\n   669→              if (!stderrLine.trim()) continue;\n   670→              try {\n   671→                const stderrData = JSON.parse(stderrLine);\n   672→                // Output formatted JSON (same formatting as stdout)\n   673→                await log(JSON.stringify(stderrData, null, 2));\n   674→                // Capture session ID from stderr too (agent sends it via stderr)\n   675→                if (!sessionId && stderrData.sessionID) {\n   676→                  sessionId = stderrData.sessionID;\n   677→                  await log(`📌 Session ID: ${sessionId}`);\n   678→                }\n   679→                // Issue #1250: Accumulate token usage during streaming (stderr)\n   680→                accumulateTokenUsage(stderrData);\n   681→                // Issue #1201: Detect error events during streaming (stderr) for reliable detection\n   682→                if (stderrData.type === 'error' || stderrData.type === 'step_error') {\n   683→                  streamingErrorDetected = true;\n   684→                  streamingErrorMessage = stderrData.message || stderrData.error || stderrLine.substring(0, 100);\n   685→                  await log(`⚠️  Error event detected in stream: ${streamingErrorMessage}`, { level: 'warning' });\n   686→                }\n   687→                // Issue #1263: Track text content for result summary (stderr)\n   688→                if (stderrData.type === 'text' && stderrData.text) {\n   689→                  lastTextContent = stderrData.text;\n   690→                } else if (stderrData.type === 'assistant' && stderrData.message?.content) {\n   691→                  const content = Array.isArray(stderrData.message.content) ? stderrData.message.content :
