Raw stdout output from agent command\n * @returns {Object} Aggregated token usage and cost data\n */\nexport const parseAgentTokenUsage = output => {\n  const usage = {\n    inputTokens: 0,\n    outputTokens: 0,\n    reasoningTokens: 0,\n    cacheReadTokens: 0,\n    cacheWriteTokens: 0,\n    totalCost: 0,\n    stepCount: 0,\n  };\n\n  // Try to parse each line as JSON (agent outputs NDJSON format)\n  const lines = output.split('\\n');\n  for (const line of lines) {\n    const trimmedLine = line.trim();\n    if (!trimmedLine || !trimmedLine.startsWith('{')) continue;\n\n    try {\n      const parsed = JSON.parse(trimmedLine);\n\n      // Look for step_finish events which contain token usage\n      if (parsed.type === 'step_finish' && parsed.part?.tokens) {\n        const tokens = parsed.part.tokens;\n        usage.stepCount++;\n\n        // Add token counts\n        if (tokens.input) usage.inputTokens += tokens.input;\n        if (tokens.output) usage.outputTokens += tokens.output;\n        if (tokens.reasoning) usage.reasoningTokens += tokens.reasoning;\n\n        // Handle cache tokens (can be in different formats)\n        if (tokens.cache) {\n          if (tokens.cache.read) usage.cacheReadTokens += tokens.cache.read;\n          if (tokens.cache.write) usage.cacheWriteTokens += tokens.cache.write;\n        }\n\n        // Add cost from step_finish (usually 0 for free models like grok-code)\n        if (parsed.part.cost !== undefined) {\n          usage.totalCost += parsed.part.cost;\n        }\n      }\n    } catch {\n      // Skip lines that aren't valid JSON\n      continue;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return usage;\n};\n\n/**\n * Helper function to get original provider name from provider identifier\n * Used for calculating public pricing estimates based on original provider prices\n * @param {string} providerId - Provider identifier (e.g., 'openai', 'anthropic', 'moonshot')\n * @returns {string} Human-readable provider name for pricing reference\n */\nconst getOriginalProviderName = providerId => {\n  if (!providerId) return null;\n\n  const providerMap = {\n    openai: 'OpenAI',\n    anthropic: 'Anthropic',\n    moonshot: 'Moonshot AI',\n    google: 'Google',\n    opencode: 'OpenCode Zen',\n    grok: 'xAI',\n  };\n\n  return providerMap[providerId] || providerId.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + providerId.slice(1);\n};\n\n/**\n * Issue #1250: Normalize model name and find base model for pricing lookup\n * Free models like \"kimi-k2.5-free\" should use pricing from base model \"kimi-k2.5\"\n *\n * @param {string} modelName - The model name (e.g., 'kimi-k2.5-free')\n * @returns {Object} Object with:\n *   - baseModelName: The base model name for pricing lookup\n *   - isFreeVariant: Whether this is a free variant\n */\nconst getBaseModelForPricing = modelName => {\n  // Known mappings for free models to their base paid versions\n  const freeToBaseMap = {\n    'kimi-k2.5-free': 'kimi-k2.5',\n    'glm-4.7-free': 'glm-4.7',\n    'minimax-m2.1-free': 'minimax-m2.1',\n    'trinity-large-preview-free': 'trinity-large-preview',\n    // Grok models don't have a paid equivalent with same name\n    // These are kept as-is since they're truly free\n  };\n\n  // Check if there's a direct mapping\n  if (freeToBaseMap[modelName]) {\n    return {\n      baseModelName: freeToBaseMap[modelName],\n      isFreeVariant: true,\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Try removing \"-free\" suffix\n  if (modelName.endsWith('-free')) {\n    return {\n      baseModelName: modelName.replace(/-free$/, ''),\n      isFreeVariant: true,\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Not a free variant\n  return {\n    baseModelName: modelName,\n    isFreeVariant: false,\n  };\n};\n\n/**\n * Calculate pricing for agent tool usage using models.dev API\n * Issue #1250: Shows actual provider (OpenCode Zen) and calculates public pricing estimate\n * based on original provider prices (Moonshot AI, OpenAI, Anthropic, etc.)\n *\n * For free models like \"kimi-k2.5-free\", this function:\n * 1. First fetches the free model info to get the model name\n * 2. Then fetches the base model (e.g., \"kimi-k2.5\") for actual pricing\n * 3. Calculates public pricing estimate based on the base model's cost\n *\n * @param {string} modelId - The model ID used (e.g., 'opencode/grok-code')\n * @param {Object} tokenUsage - Token usage data from parseAgentTokenUsage\n * @returns {Object} Pricing information with:\n *   - provider: Always \"OpenCode Zen\" (actual provider)\n *   - originalProvider: The original model provider for pricing reference\n *   - totalCostUSD: Public pricing estimate based on original provider prices\n *   - opencodeCost: Actual billed cost from OpenCode Zen (free for most models)\n */\nexport const calculateAgentPricing = async (modelId, tokenUsage) => {\n  // Extract the model name from provider/model format\n  // e.g., 'opencode/grok-code' -> 'grok-code'\n  const modelName = modelId.includes('/') ? modelId.split('/').pop() : modelId;\n\n  // Extract provider from model ID to determine original provider for pricing\n  const providerFromModel = modelId.includes('/') ? modelId.split('/')[0] : null;\n\n  // Get original provider name for pricing reference\n  let originalProvider = getOriginalProviderName(providerFromModel);\n\n  try {\n    // Fetch model info from models.dev API\n    let modelInfo = await fetchModelInfo(modelName);\n\n    // Issue #1250: Check if model has zero pricing (free model from OpenCode Zen)\n    // If so, look up the base model for actual public pricing estimate\n    const { baseModelName, isFreeVariant } = getBaseModelForPricing(modelName);\n    let baseModelInfo = null;\n    let pricingCost = modelInfo?.cost;\n\n    if (modelInfo && modelInfo.cost && modelInfo.cost.input === 0 && modelInfo.cost.output === 0 && baseModelName !== modelName) {\n      // This is a free model with zero pricing - look up base model for public pricing\n      baseModelInfo = await fetchModelInfo(baseModelName);\n      if (baseModelInfo && baseModelInfo.cost) {\n        // Use base model pricing for public estimate\n        pricingCost = baseModelInfo.cost;\n        // Update original provider from base model if available\n        if (baseModelInfo.provider && !originalProvider) {\n          originalProvider = baseModelInfo.provider;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (modelInfo || baseModelInfo) {\n      const effectiveModelInfo = modelInfo || baseModelInfo;\n      const cost = pricingCost || { input: 0, output: 0, cache_read: 0, cache_write: 0, reasoning: 0 };\n\n      // Calculate public pricing estimate based on original provider prices\n      // Prices are per 1M tokens, so divide by 1,000,000\n      // All priced components from models.dev: input, output, cache_read, cache_write, reasoning\n      const inputCost = (tokenUsage.inputTokens * (cost.input || 0)) / 1_000_000;\n      const outputCost = (tokenUsage.outputTokens * (cost.output || 0)) / 1_000_000;\n      const cacheReadCost = (tokenUsage.cacheReadTokens * (cost.cache_read || 0)) / 1_000_000;\n      const cacheWriteCost = (tokenUsage.cacheWriteTokens * (cost.cache_write || 0)) / 1_000_000;\n      const reasoningCost = (tokenUsage.reasoningTokens * (cost.reasoning || 0)) / 1_000_000;\n\n      const totalCost = inputCost + outputCost + cacheReadCost + cacheWriteCost + reasoningCost;\n\n      // Determine if this is a free model from OpenCode Zen\n      // Models accessed via OpenCode Zen are free, regardless of original provider pricing\n      const isOpencodeFreeModel = providerFromModel === 'opencode' || isFreeVariant || modelName.toLowerCase().includes('free') || modelName.toLowerCase().includes('grok') || providerFromModel === 'moonshot' || providerFromModel === 'openai' || providerFromModel === 'anthropic';\n\n      // Use base model's provider for original provider reference if available\n      const effectiveOriginalProvider = baseModelInfo?.provider || originalProvider || effectiveModelInfo?.provider || null;\n\n      return {\n        modelId,\n        modelName: effectiveModelInfo?.name || modelName,\n        // Issue #1250: Always show OpenCode Zen as actual provider\n        provider: 'OpenCode Zen',\n        // Store original provider for reference in pricing display\n        originalProvider: effectiveOriginalProvider,\n        pricing: {\n          inputPerMillion: cost.input || 0,\n          outputPerMillion: cost.output || 0,\n          cacheReadPerMillion: cost.cache_read || 0,\n          cacheWritePerMillion: cost.cache_write || 0,\n          reasoningPerMillion: cost.reasoning || 0,\n        },\n        tokenUsage,\n        breakdown: {\n          input: inputCost,\n          output: outputCost,\n          cacheRead: cacheReadCost,\n          cacheWrite: cacheWriteCost,\n          reasoning: reasoningCost,\n        },\n        // Public pricing estimate based on original/base model prices\n        totalCostUSD: totalCost,\n        // Actual cost from OpenCode Zen (free for supported models)\n        opencodeCost: isOpencodeFreeModel ? 0 : totalCost,\n        // Keep for backward compatibility - indicates if the accessed model has zero pricing\n        isFreeModel: modelInfo?.cost?.input === 0 && modelInfo?.cost?.output === 0,\n        // New flag to indicate if OpenCode Zen provides this model for free\n        isOpencodeFreeModel,\n        // Issue #1250: Include base model info for transparency\n        baseModelName: baseModelName !== modelName ? baseModelName : null,\n      };\n    }\n    // Model not found in API, return what we have\n    return {\n      modelId,\n      modelName,\n      provider: 'OpenCode Zen',\n      originalProvider,\n      tokenUsage,\n      totalCostUSD: null,\n      opencodeCost: 0, // OpenCode Zen is free\n      isOpencodeFreeModel: true,\n      error: 'Model not found in models.dev API',\n    };\n  } catch (error) {\n    // Error fetching pricing, return with error info\n    return {\n      modelId,\n      modelName,\n      provider: 'OpenCode Zen',\n      originalProvider,\n      tokenUsage,\n      totalCostUSD: null,\n      opencodeCost: 0, // OpenCode Zen is free\n      isOpencodeFreeModel: true,\n      error: error.message,\n    };\n  }\n};\n\n// Model mapping to translate aliases to full model IDs for Agent\n// Agent uses OpenCode Zen's JSON interface and models\n// Issue #1185: Free models use opencode/ prefix (not openai/)\nexport const mapModelToId = model => {\n  const modelMap = {\n    grok: 'opencode/grok-code',\n    'grok-code': 'opencode/grok-code',\n    'grok-code-fast-1': 'opencode/grok-code',\n    'big-pickle': 'opencode/big-pickle',\n    'gpt-5-nano': 'opencode/gpt-5-nano',\n    sonnet: 'anthropic/claude-3-5-sonnet',\n    haiku: 'anthropic/claude-3-5-haiku',\n    opus: 'anthropic/claude-3-opus',\n    'gemini-3-pro': 'google/gemini-3-pro',\n    // Free models mapping for issue #1250\n    'kimi-k2.5-free': 'moonshot/kimi-k2.5-free',\n    'gpt-4o-mini': 'openai/gpt-4o-mini',\n    'gpt-4o': 'openai/gpt-4o',\n    'claude-3.5-haiku': 'anthropic/claude-3.5-haiku',\n    'claude-3.5-sonnet': 'anthropic/claude-3.5-sonnet',\n  };\n\n  // Return mapped model ID if it's an alias, otherwise return as-is\n  return modelMap[model] || model;\n};\n\n// Function to validate Agent connection\nexport const validateAgentConnection = async (model = 'grok-code-fast-1') => {\n  // Map model alias to full ID\n  const mappedModel = mapModelToId(model);\n\n  // Retry configuration\n  const maxRetries = 3;\n  let retryCount = 0;\n\n  const attemptValidation = async () => {\n    try {\n      if (retryCount === 0) {\n        await log('🔍 Validating Agent connection...');\n      } else {\n        await log(`🔄 Retry attempt ${retryCount}/${maxRetries} for Agent validation...`);\n      }\n\n      // Check if Agent CLI is installed and get version\n      try {\n        const versionResult = await $`timeout ${Math.floor(timeouts.opencodeCli / 1000)} agent --version`;\n        if (versionResult.code === 0) {\n          const version = versionResult.stdout?.toString().trim();\n          if (retryCount === 0) {\n            await log(`📦 Agent CLI version: ${version}`);\n          }\n        }\n      } catch (versionError) {\n        if (retryCount === 0) {\n          await log(`⚠️  Agent CLI version check failed (${versionError.code}), proceeding with connection test...`);\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Test basic Agent functionality with a simple \"hi\" message\n      // Agent uses the same JSON interface as OpenCode\n      const testResult = await $`printf \"hi\" | timeout ${Math.floor(timeouts.opencodeCli / 1000)} agent --model ${mappedModel}`;\n\n      if (testResult.code !== 0) {\n        const stderr = testResult.stderr?.toString() || '';\n\n        if (stderr.includes('auth') || stderr.includes('login')) {\n          await log('❌ Agent authentication failed', { level: 'error' });\n          await log('   💡 Note: Agent uses OpenCode models. For premium models, you may need: opencode auth', {\n            level: 'error',\n          });\n          return false;\n        }\n\n        await log(`❌ Agent validation failed with exit code ${testResult.code}`, { level: 'error' });\n        if (stderr) await log(`   Error: ${stderr.trim()}`, { level: 'error' });\n        return false;\n      }\n\n      // Success\n      await log('✅ Agent connection validated successfully');\n      return true;\n    } catch (error) {\n      await log(`❌ Failed to validate Agent connection: ${error.message}`, { level: 'error' });\n      await log('   💡 Make sure @link-assistant/agent is installed globally: bun install -g @link-assistant/agent', {\n        level: 'error',\n      });\n      return false;\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Start the validation\n  return await attemptValidation();\n};\n\n// Function to handle Agent runtime switching (if applicable)\nexport const handleAgentRuntimeSwitch = async () => {\n  // Agent is run via Bun as a CLI tool, runtime switching may not be applicable\n  // This function can be used for any runtime-specific configurations if needed\n  await log('ℹ️  Agent runtime handling not required for this operation');\n};\n\n// Main function to execute Agent with prompts and settings\nexport const executeAgent = async params => {\n  const { issueUrl, issueNumber, prNumber, prUrl, branchName, tempDir, workspaceTmpDir, isContinueMode, mergeStateStatus, forkedRepo, feedbackLines, forkActionsUrl, owner, repo, argv, log, formatAligned, getResourceSnapshot, agentPath = 'agent', $ } = params;\n\n  // Import prompt building functions from agent.prompts.lib.mjs\n  const { buildUserPrompt, buildSystemPrompt } = await import('./agent.prompts.lib.mjs');\n\n  // Check if the model supports vision using models.dev API\n  const mappedModel = mapModelToId(argv.model);\n  const modelSupportsVision = await checkModelVisionCapability(mappedModel);\n  if (argv.verbose) {\n    await log(`👁️  Model vision capability: ${modelSupportsVision ? 'supported' : 'not supported'}`, { verbose: true });\n  }\n\n  // Build the user prompt\n  const prompt = buildUserPrompt({\n    issueUrl,\n    issueNumber,\n    prNumber,\n    prUrl,\n    branchName,\n    tempDir,\n    workspaceTmpDir,\n    isContinueMode,\n    mergeStateStatus,\n    forkedRepo,\n    feedbackLines,\n    forkActionsUrl,\n    owner,\n    repo,\n    argv,\n  });\n\n  // Build the system prompt\n  const systemPrompt = buildSystemPrompt({\n    owner,\n    repo,\n    issueNumber,\n    prNumber,\n    branchName,\n    tempDir,\n    workspaceTmpDir,\n    isContinueMode,\n    forkedRepo,\n    argv,\n    modelSupportsVision,\n  });\n\n  // Log prompt details in verbose mode\n  if (argv.verbose) {\n    await log('\\n📝 Final prompt structure:', { verbose: true });\n    await log(`   Characters: ${prompt.length}`, { verbose: true });\n    await log(`   System prompt characters: ${systemPrompt.length}`, { verbose: true });\n    if (feedbackLines && feedbackLines.length > 0) {\n      await log('   Feedback info: Included', { verbose: true });\n    }\n\n    if (argv.dryRun) {\n      await log('\\n📋 User prompt content:', { verbose: true });\n      await log('---BEGIN USER PROMPT---', { verbose: true });\n      await log(prompt, { verbose: true });\n      await log('---END USER PROMPT---', { verbose: true });\n      await log('\\n📋 System prompt content:', { verbose: true });\n      await log('---BEGIN SYSTEM PROMPT---', { verbose: true });\n      await log(systemPrompt, { verbose: true });\n      await log('---END SYSTEM PROMPT---', { verbose: true });\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Execute the Agent command\n  return await executeAgentCommand({\n    tempDir,\n    branchName,\n    prompt,\n    systemPrompt,\n    argv,\n    log,\n    formatAligned,\n    getResourceSnapshot,\n    forkedRepo,\n    feedbackLines,\n    agentPath,\n    $,\n  });\n};\n\nexport const executeAgentCommand = async params => {\n  const { tempDir, branchName, prompt, systemPrompt, argv, log, formatAligned, getResourceSnapshot, forkedRepo, feedbackLines, agentPath, $ } = params;\n\n  // Retry configuration\n  const maxRetries = 3;\n  let retryCount = 0;\n\n  const executeWithRetry = async () => {\n    // Execute agent command from the cloned repository directory\n    if (retryCount === 0) {\n      await log(`\\n${formatAligned('🤖', 'Executing Agent:', argv.model.toUpperCase())}`);\n    } else {\n      await log(`\\n${formatAligned('🔄', 'Retry attempt:', `${retryCount}/${maxRetries}`)}`);\n    }\n\n    if (argv.verbose) {\n      await log(`   Model: ${argv.model}`, { verbose: true });\n      await log(`   Working directory: ${tempDir}`, { verbose: true });\n      await log(`   Branch: ${branchName}`, { verbose: true });\n      await log(`   Prompt length: ${prompt.length} chars`, { verbose: true });\n      await log(`   System prompt length: ${systemPrompt.length} chars`, { verbose: true });\n      if (feedbackLines && feedbackLines.length > 0) {\n        await log(`   Feedback info included: Yes (${feedbackLines.length} lines)`, { verbose: true });\n      } else {\n        await log('   Feedback info included: No', { verbose: true });\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Take resource snapshot before execution\n    const resourcesBefore = await getResourceSnapshot();\n    await log('📈 System resources before execution:', { verbose: true });\n    await log(`   Memory: ${resourcesBefore.memory.split('\\n')[1]}`, { verbose: true });\n    await log(`   Load: ${resourcesBefore.load}`, { verbose: true });\n\n    // Build Agent command\n    let execCommand;\n\n    // Map model alias to full ID\n    const mappedModel = mapModelToId(argv.model);\n\n    // Build agent command arguments\n    let agentArgs = `--model ${mappedModel}`;\n\n    // Propagate verbose flag to agent for detailed debugging output\n    if (argv.verbose) {\n      agentArgs += ' --verbose';\n    }\n\n    // Agent supports stdin in both plain text and JSON format\n    // We'll combine system and user prompts into a single message\n    const combinedPrompt = systemPrompt ? `${systemPrompt}\\n\\n${prompt}` : prompt;\n\n    // Write the combined prompt to a file for piping\n    // Use OS temporary directory instead of repository workspace to avoid polluting the repo\n    const promptFile = path.join(os.tmpdir(), `agent_prompt_${Date.now()}_${process.pid}.txt`);\n    await fs.writeFile(promptFile, combinedPrompt);\n\n    // Build the full command - pipe the prompt file to agent\n    const fullCommand = `(cd \"${tempDir}\" && cat \"${promptFile}\" | ${agentPath} ${agentArgs})`;\n\n    await log(`\\n${formatAligned('📝', 'Raw command:', '')}`);\n    await log(`${fullCommand}`);\n    await log('');\n\n    try {\n      // Pipe the prompt file to agent via stdin\n      // Use agentArgs which includes --model and optionally --verbose\n      execCommand = $({\n        cwd: tempDir,\n        mirror: false,\n      })`cat ${promptFile} | ${agentPath} ${agentArgs}`;\n\n      await log(`${formatAligned('📋', 'Command details:', '')}`);\n      await log(formatAligned('📂', 'Working directory:', tempDir, 2));\n      await log(formatAligned('🌿', 'Branch:', branchName, 2));\n      await log(formatAligned('🤖', 'Model:', `Agent ${argv.model.toUpperCase()}`, 2));\n      if (argv.fork && forkedRepo) {\n        await log(formatAligned('🍴', 'Fork:', forkedRepo, 2));\n      }\n\n      await log(`\\n${formatAligned('▶️', 'Streaming output:', '')}\\n`);\n\n      let exitCode = 0;\n      let sessionId = null;\n      let limitReached = false;\n      let limitResetTime = null;\n      let lastMessage = '';\n      let lastTextContent = ''; // Issue #1263: Track last text content for result summary\n      let fullOutput = ''; // Collect all output for error detection (kept for backward compatibility)\n      // Issue #1201: Track error events detected during streaming for reliable error detection\n      // Post-hoc detection on fullOutput can miss errors if NDJSON lines get concatenated without newlines\n      let streamingErrorDetected = false;\n      let streamingErrorMessage = null;\n      // Issue #1276: Track successful completion events to clear error flags\n      // When agent emits session.idle or disposal events, it means it recovered and completed successfully\n      let agentCompletedSuccessfully = false;\n      // Issue #1250: Accumulate token usage during streaming instead of parsing fullOutput later\n      // This fixes the issue where NDJSON lines get concatenated without newlines, breaking JSON.parse\n      const streamingTokenUsage = {\n        inputTokens: 0,\n        outputTokens: 0,\n        reasoningTokens: 0,\n        cacheReadTokens: 0,\n        cacheWriteTokens: 0,\n        totalCost: 0,\n        stepCount: 0,\n      };\n      // Helper to accumulate tokens from step_finish events during streaming\n      const accumulateTokenUsage = data => {\n        if (data.type === 'step_finish' && data.part?.tokens) {\n          const tokens = data.part.tokens;\n          streamingTokenUsage.stepCount++;\n          if (tokens.input) streamingTokenUsage.inputTokens += tokens.input;\n          if (tokens.output) streamingTokenUsage.outputTokens += tokens.output;\n          if (tokens.reasoning) streamingTokenUsage.reasoningTokens += tokens.reasoning;\n          if (tokens.cache) {\n            if (tokens.cache.read) streamingTokenUsage.cacheReadTokens += tokens.cache.read;\n            if (tokens.cache.write) streamingTokenUsage.cacheWriteTokens += tokens.cache.write;\n          }\n          if (data.part.cost !== undefined) {\n            streamingTokenUsage.totalCost += data.part.cost;\n          }\n        }\n      };\n\n      for await (const chunk of execCommand.stream()) {\n        if (chunk.type === 'stdout') {\n          const output = chunk.data.toString();\n          // Split output into individual lines for NDJSON parsing\n          // Agent outputs NDJSON (newline-delimited JSON) format where each line is a separate JSON object\n          // This allows us to parse each event independently and extract structured data like session IDs\n          const lines = output.split('\\n');\n          for (const line of lines) {\n            if (!line.trim()) continue;\n            try {\n              const data = JSON.parse(line);\n              // Output formatted JSON\n              await log(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));\n              // Capture session ID from the first message\n              if (!sessionId && data.sessionID) {\n                sessionId = data.sessionID;\n                await log(`📌 Session ID: ${sessionId}`);\n              }\n              // Issue #1250: Accumulate token usage during streaming\n              accumulateTokenUsage(data);\n              // Issue #1201: Detect error events during streaming for reliable detection\n              if (data.type === 'error' || data.type === 'step_error') {\n                streamingErrorDetected = true;\n                streamingErrorMessage = data.message || data.error || line.substring(0, 100);\n                await log(`⚠️  Error event detected in stream: ${streamingErrorMessage}`, { level: 'warning' });\n              }\n              // Issue #1263: Track text content for result summary\n              // Agent outputs text via 'text', 'assistant', or 'message' type events\n              if (data.type === 'text' && data.text) {\n                lastTextContent = data.text;\n              } else if (data.type === 'assistant' && data.message?.content) {\n                // Extract text from assistant message content\n                const content = Array.isArray(data.message.content) ? data.message.content : [data.message.content];\n                for (const item of content) {\n                  if (item.type === 'text' && item.text) {\n                    lastTextContent = item.text;\n                  }\n                }\n              } else if (data.type === 'message' && data.content) {\n                // Direct message content\n                if (typeof data.content === 'string') {\n                  lastTextContent = data.content;\n                } else if (Array.isArray(data.content)) {\n                  for (const item of data.content) {\n                    if (item.type === 'text' && item.text) {\n                      lastTextContent = item.text;\n                    }\n                  }\n                }\n              } else if (data.type === 'result' && data.result) {\n                // Explicit result message (like Claude outputs)\n                lastTextContent = data.result;\n              }\n              // Issue #1276: Detect successful completion events\n              // When agent emits session.idle or log with \"exiting loop\" message, it completed successfully\n              // This means any previous error events were recovered from (e.g., timeout then retry)\n              if (data.type === 'session.idle' || (data.type === 'log' && data.message === 'exiting loop')) {\n                agentCompletedSuccessfully = true;\n              }\n            } catch {\n              // Not JSON - log as plain text\n              await log(line);\n            }\n          }\n          lastMessage = output;\n          fullOutput += output; // Collect for both pricing calculation and error detection\n        }\n\n        if (chunk.type === 'stderr') {\n          const errorOutput = chunk.data.toString();\n          if (errorOutput) {\n            // Agent sends all output (including verbose logs and structured events) to stderr\n            // Process each line as NDJSON, same as stdout handling\n            const stderrLines = errorOutput.split('\\n');\n            for (const stderrLine of stderrLines) {\n              if (!stderrLine.trim()) continue;\n              try {\n                const stderrData = JSON.parse(stderrLine);\n                // Output formatted JSON (same formatting as stdout)\n                await log(JSON.stringify(stderrData, null, 2));\n                // Capture session ID from stderr too (agent sends it via stderr)\n                if (!sessionId && stderrData.sessionID) {\n                  sessionId = stderrData.sessionID;\n                  await log(`📌 Session ID: ${sessionId}`);\n                }\n                // Issue #1250: Accumulate token usage during streaming (stderr)\n                accumulateTokenUsage(stderrData);\n                // Issue #1201: Detect error events during streaming (stderr) for reliable detection\n                if (stderrData.type === 'error' || stderrData.type === 'step_error') {\n                  streamingErrorDetected = true;\n                  streamingErrorMessage = stderrData.message || stderrData.error || stderrLine.substring(0, 100);\n                  await log(`⚠️  Error event detected in stream: ${streamingErrorMessage}`, { level: 'warning' });\n                }\n                // Issue #1263: Track text content for result summary (stderr)\n                if (stderrData.type === 'text' && stderrData.text) {\n                  lastTextContent = stderrData.text;\n                } else if (stderrData.type === 'assistant' && stderrData.message?.content) {\n                  const content = Array.isArray(stderrData.message.content) ? stderrData.message.content : [stderrData.message.content];\n                  for (const item of content) {\n                    if (item.type === 'text' && item.text) {\n                      lastTextContent = item.text;\n                    }\n                  }\n                } else if (stderrData.type === 'message' && stderrData.content) {\n                  if (typeof stderrData.content === 'string') {\n                    lastTextContent = stderrData.content;\n                  } else if (Array.isArray(stderrData.content)) {\n                    for (const item of stderrData.content) {\n                      if (item.type === 'text' && item.text) {\n                        lastTextContent = item.text;\n                      }\n                    }\n                  }\n                } else if (stderrData.type === 'result' && stderrData.result) {\n                  lastTextContent = stderrData.result;\n                }\n                // Issue #1276: Detect successful completion events (stderr)\n                // When agent emits session.idle or log with \"exiting loop\" message, it completed successfully\n                if (stderrData.type === 'session.idle' || (stderrData.type === 'log' && stderrData.message === 'exiting loop')) {\n                  agentCompletedSuccessfully = true;\n                }\n              } catch {\n                // Not JSON - log as plain text\n                await log(stderrLine);\n              }\n            }\n            // Also collect stderr for error detection\n            fullOutput += errorOutput;\n          }\n        } else if (chunk.type === 'exit') {\n          exitCode = chunk.code;\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Simplified error detection for agent tool\n      // Issue #886: Trust exit code - agent now properly returns code 1 on errors with JSON error response\n      // Don't scan output for error patterns as this causes false positives during normal operation\n      // (e.g., AI executing bash commands that produce \"Permission denied\" warnings but succeed)\n      //\n      // Error detection is now based on:\n      // 1. Non-zero exit code (agent returns 1 on errors)\n      // 2. Explicit JSON error messages from agent (type: \"error\")\n      // 3. Usage limit detection (handled separately)\n      const detectAgentErrors = stdoutOutput => {\n        const lines = stdoutOutput.split('\\n');\n\n        for (const line of lines) {\n          if (!line.trim()) continue;\n\n          try {\n            const msg = JSON.parse(line);\n\n            // Check for explicit error message types from agent\n            if (msg.type === 'error' || msg.type === 'step_error') {\n              return { detected: true, type: 'AgentError', match: msg.message || msg.error || line.substring(0, 100) };\n            }\n          } catch {\n            // Not JSON - ignore for error detection\n            continue;\n          }\n        }\n\n        return { detected: false };\n      };\n\n      // Only check for JSON error messages, not pattern matching in output\n      const outputError = detectAgentErrors(fullOutput);\n\n      // Issue #1276: Clear streaming error detection if agent completed successfully\n      // When an error occurs during execution (e.g., timeout) but the agent recovers and completes,\n      // we should NOT treat it as a failure. The exit code is the authoritative success indicator.\n      // Check for: exit code 0 AND (completion event detected OR no streaming error)\n      if (exitCode === 0 && (agentCompletedSuccessfully || !streamingErrorDetected)) {\n        // Agent exited successfully - clear any streaming errors that were recovered from\n        if (streamingErrorDetected && agentCompletedSuccessfully) {\n          await log(`ℹ️  Agent recovered from earlier error and completed successfully`, { verbose: true });\n        }\n        streamingErrorDetected = false;\n        streamingErrorMessage = null;\n      }\n\n      // Issue #1201: Use streaming detection as primary, post-hoc as fallback\n      // Streaming detection is more reliable because it parses each JSON line as it arrives,\n      // avoiding issues where NDJSON lines get concatenated without newline delimiters in fullOutput\n      if (!outputError.detected && streamingErrorDetected) {\n        outputError.detected = true;\n        outputError.type = 'AgentError';\n        outputError.match = streamingErrorMessage;\n      }\n\n      // Issue #1258: Fallback pattern match for error detection\n      // When JSON parsing fails (e.g., multi-line pretty-printed JSON in logs),\n      // we need to detect error patterns in the raw output string\n      // Issue #1290: Skip fallback when agent completed successfully with exit code 0\n      // The fallback can cause false positives when error events (like AI_JSONParseError)\n      // appear in the output but the agent recovered and completed successfully\n      if (!outputError.detected && !streamingErrorDetected && !(exitCode === 0 && agentCompletedSuccessfully)) {\n        // Check for error type patterns in raw output (handles pretty-printed JSON)\n        const errorTypePatterns = [\n          { pattern: '\"type\": \"error\"', type: 'AgentError' },\n          { pattern: '\"type\":\"error\"', type: 'AgentError' },\n          { pattern: '\"type\": \"step_error\"', type: 'AgentStepError' },\n          { pattern: '\"type\":\"step_error\"', type: 'AgentStepError' },\n        ];\n\n        for (const { pattern, type } of errorTypePatterns) {\n          if (fullOutput.includes(pattern)) {\n            outputError.detected = true;\n            outputError.type = type;\n            // Issue #1276: Try to extract the error message from the output\n            // First try \"error\" field (agent error format), then \"message\" field (generic format)\n            // Find the error closest to the \"type\": \"error\" pattern for more accurate extraction\n            const patternIndex = fullOutput.indexOf(pattern);\n            const relevantOutput = patternIndex >= 0 ? fullOutput.substring(patternIndex) : fullOutput;\n            // Look for \"error\" or \"message\" field near the error type pattern\n            const errorFieldMatch = relevantOutput.match(/\"error\":\\s*\"([^\"]+)\"/);\n            const messageFieldMatch = relevantOutput.match(/\"message\":\\s*\"([^\"]+)\"/);\n            // Prefer \"error\" field over \"message\" for agent error events\n            outputError.match = errorFieldMatch ? errorFieldMatch[1] : messageFieldMatch ? messageFieldMatch[1] : `Error event detected in output (fallback pattern match for ${pattern})`;\n            await log(`⚠️  Error event detected via fallback pattern match: ${outputError.match}`, { level: 'warning' });\n            break;\n          }\n        }\n\n        // Also check for known critical error patterns that indicate failure\n        if (!outputError.detected) {\n          const criticalErrorPatterns = [\n            { pattern: 'AI_RetryError:', extract: /AI_RetryError:\\s*(.+?)(?:\\n|$)/ },\n            { pattern: 'UnhandledRejection', extract: /\"errorType\":\\s*\"UnhandledRejection\"/ },\n            { pattern: 'Failed after 3 attempts', extract: /Failed after \\d+ attempts[^\"]*/ },\n          ];\n\n log(`⚠️  Critical error pattern detected via fallback: ${outputError.match}`, { level: 'warning' });\n              break;\n            }\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (exitCode !== 0 || outputError.detected) {\n        // Build JSON error structure for consistent error reporting\n        const errorInfo = {\n          type: 'error',\n          exitCode,\n limitResetTime: null,\n        };\n\n        // Check for usage limit errors first (more specific)\n        // Issue #1287: Check multiple sources for usage limit detection:\n        // 1. lastMessage true;\n          limitResetTime = limitInfo.resetTime;\n          errorInfo.limitReached = true;\n          errorInfo.limitResetTime = limitResetTime;\n          errorInfo.errorType = 'UsageLimit';\n\n          // Format and display user-friendly message\n          const messageLines = formatUsageLimitMessage({\n            tool: 'Agent',\n            resetTime: Solomonoff 1956.  Alan Turing discussed the centrality of learning as early as 1950, in his classic paper \\\"Computing Machinery and Intelligence\\\".[120] In 1956, at the original Dartmouth AI summer conference, Ray Solomonoff wrote a report on unsupervised probabilistic machine learning: \\\"An Inductive Inference Machine\\\".[121]  This is a form of Tom Mitchell's widely quoted definition of machine learning: \\\"A computer program is set to learn from an experience E with respect to some task T and some performance measure P if its performance on T as measured by P improves with experience E.\\\"  Learning: * ACM 1998, I.2.6, * Russell & Norvig 2003, pp. 649–788, * Poole, Mackworth & Goebel 1998, pp. 397–438, * Luger & Stubblefield 2004, pp. 385–542, * Nilsson 1998, chpt. 3.3, 10.3, 17.5, 20  Jordan, M. The Turing test: Turing's original publication: * Turing 1950 Historical influence and philosophical implications: * Haugeland 1985, pp. 6–9 * Crevier 1993, p. 24 * McCorduck 2004, pp. 70–71 * Russell & Norvig 2003, pp. 2–3 and 948  Dartmouth proposal: * McCarthy et al. 1955 (the original proposal) * Crevier 1993, p. 49 (historical significance)  The physical symbol systems hypothesis: * Newell & Simon 1976, p. 116 * McCorduck 2004, p. 153 * Russell & Norvig 2003, p. 18  Dreyfus 1992, p. 156.  Dreyfus criticized the necessary condition of the physical symbol system hypothesis, which he called the \\\"psychological assumption\\\": \\\"The mind can be viewed as a device operating on bits of information according to formal rules.\\\"[206]  Dreyfus' critique of artificial intelligence: * Dreyfus 1972, Dreyfus & Dreyfus 1986 * Crevier 1993, pp. 120–132 * McCorduck 2004, pp. 211–239 * Russell & Norvig 2003, pp. 950–952,  Gödel 1951: in this lecture, Kurt Gödel uses the incompleteness theorem to arrive at the following disjunction: (a) the human mind is not a consistent finite machine, or (b) there exist Diophantine equations for which it cannot decide whether solutions exist. Gödel finds (b) implausible, and thus seems to have believed the human mind was not equivalent to a finite machine, i.e., its power exceeded that of any finite machine. He recognized that this was only a conjecture, since one could never disprove (b). Yet he considered the disjunctive conclusion to be a \\\"certain fact\\\". isUsageLimitError(message) {\n    29→  if (!message || typeof message !== 'string') {\n    30→    return false;\n    31→  }\n    32→\n    33→  const lowerMessage = message.toLowerCase();\n    34→\n    35→  // Check for specific usage limit patterns\n    36→  // Supports both plain string patterns (checked via .includes()) and RegExp patterns\n    37→  const patterns = [\n    38→    // Generic\n    39→    \"you've hit your usage limit\",\n    40→    'hit your usage limit',\n    41→    'you have exceeded your rate limit',\n    42→    'usage limit reached',\n    43→    'usage limit exceeded',\n    44→    'rate_limit_exceeded',\n    45→    'rate limit exceeded',\n    46→    'limit reached',\n    47→    'limit has been reached',\n    48→    // Provider-specific phrasings we've seen in the wild\n    49→    'session limit reached', // Claude\n    50→    'weekly limit reached', // Claude\n    51→    'daily limit reached',\n    52→    'monthly limit reached',\n    53→    'billing hard limit',\n    54→    'please try again at', // Codex/OpenCode style\n    55→    'available again at',\n    56→    // Claude shows: \"∙ resets 5am\" or \"resets Jan 15, 8am\"\n    57→    // Issue #1290: Use regex to avoid false positives when \"resets\" appears in code output\n    58→    // (e.g., \"loads a shell and resets\", \"Also resets drag start\")\n    59→    // Only match \"resets\" when followed by a time-like pattern (digit or month name)\n    60→    /resets\\s+(?:(?:at\\s+)?[0-9]|(?:Jan|Feb|Mar|Apr|May|Jun|Jul|Aug|Sep|Oct|Nov|Dec))/i,\n    61→    // Agent/OpenCode Zen specific - issue #1287\n    62→    'freeusagelimiterror', // Agent JSON error type\n    63→  ];\n    64→\n    65→  return patterns.some(pattern => {\n    66→    if (pattern instanceof RegExp) {\n    67→      return pattern.test(lowerMessage);\n    68→    }\n    69→    return lowerMessage.includes(pattern);\n    70→  });\n    71→}\n    72→\n    73→/**\n    74→ * Extract timezone from usage limit error message\n    75→ *\n    76→ * Extracts IANA timezone identifiers like \"Europe/Berlin\", \"UTC\", \"America/New_York\"\n    77→ * from messages like \"resets Jan 15, 8am (Europe/Berlin)\"\n    78→ *\n    79→ * @param {string} message - Error message to analyze\n    80→ * @returns {string|null} - Timezone string or null if not found\n    81→ */\n    82→export function extractTimezone(message) {\n    83→  if (!message || typeof message !== 'string') {\n    84→    return null;\n    85→  }\n    86→\n    87→  // Pattern: (Timezone) - matches IANA timezone format or \"UTC\"\n    88→  // IANA format: Continent/City or Continent/Region/City\n    89→  const timezoneMatch = message.match(/\\(([A-Za-z_]+(?:\\/[A-Za-z_]+){0,2})\\)/);\n    90→  if (timezoneMatch) {\n    91→    const tz = (testDate.isValid()) {\n    96→        return tz;\n    97→      }\n    98→    } catch {\n    99→      // Invalid timezone, return null\n   100→    }\n   101→  }\n   102→\n   103→  return null;\n   104→}\n   105→\n   106→/**\n   107→ * Extract reset time from usage limit error message\n   108→ *\n   109→ * Supports both time-only formats (5-hour limits) and date+time formats (weekly limits):\n   110→ * - \"resets 10pm\" → \"10:00 PM\"\n   111→ * - \"resets Jan 15, 8am\" → \"Jan 15, 8:00 AM\"\n   112→ *\n   113→ * @param {string} message - Error message to analyze\n   114→ * @returns {string|null} - Reset time string (e.g., \"12:16 PM\" or \"Jan 15, 8:00 AM\") or null if not found\n   115→ */\n   116→export function extractResetTime(message) {\n   117→  if (!message || typeof message !== 'string') {\n   118→    return null;\n   119→  }\n   120→\n   121→  // Normalize whitespace for easier matching\n   122→  const normalized = message.replace(/\\s+/g, ' ');\n   123→\n   124→  // Pattern 0: Weekly limit with date - \"resets Jan 15, 8am\" or \"resets January 15, 8:00am\"\n   125→  // This pattern must come first to avoid partial matches by time-only patterns\n   126→  const monthPattern = '(?:Jan(?:uary)?|Feb(?:ruary)?|Mar(?:ch)?|Apr(?:il)?|May|Jun(?:e)?|Jul(?:y)?|Aug(?:ust)?|Sep(?:t(?:ember)?)?|Oct(?:ober)?|Nov(?:ember)?|Dec(?:ember)?)';\n   127→  const resetsWithDateRegex = new RegExp(`resets\\\\s+(${monthPattern})\\\\s+(\\\\d{1,2}),?\\\\s+([0-9]{1,2})(?::([0-9]{2}))?\\\\s*([ap]m)`, 'i');\n   128→  const resetsWithDate = normalized.match(resetsWithDateRegex);\n   129→  if (resetsWithDate) {\n   130→    const month = resetsWithDate[1];\n   131→    const day = resetsWithDate[2];\n   132→    const hour = \"Sept\" to \"Sep\" for dayjs compatibility\n  const normalized = timeStr.replace(/\\bSept\\b/gi, 'Sep');\n\n  // Try date+time formats using dayjs custom parse\n  // dayjs uses: MMM=Jan, MMMM=January, D=day, h=12-hour, mm=minutes, A=AM/PM\n  const dateTimeFormats = ['MMM D, h:mm A', 'MMMM D, h:mm A'];\n\n  for (const format of dateTimeFormats) {\n    let parsed;\n    if (tz) {\n = dayjs(normalized, format);\n    }\n\n    if (parsed.isValid()) {\n      // dayjs parses without year, so it defaults to current year\n      // If the date is in the past, assume next year\n      if (parsed.isBefore(now)) {\n        parsed = parsed.add(1, 'year');\n      }\n      return parsed;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Try time-only format: \"8:00 PM\" or \"8:00PM\"\n  const timeOnlyFormats = ['h:mm A', 'h:mmA'];\n\n  for (const format of timeOnlyFormats) {\n    let parsed;\n    if (tz) {\n      try {\n        parsed = dayjs.tz(normalized, format, tz);\n      } catch {\n        parsed = dayjs(normalized, format);\n      }\n    } else {\n      parsed = dayjs(normalized, format);\n    }\n\n    if (parsed.isValid()) {\n      // For time-only, set to today's date\n      parsed = parsed.year(now.year()).month(now.month()).date(now.date());\n\n      // Re-apply timezone after setting date components\n      if (tz) {\n        try {\n          const dateStr = parsed.format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm');\n          parsed = dayjs.tz(dateStr, tz);\n        } catch {\n          // Keep the parsed value\n        }\n      }\n\n      // If the time is in the past today, assume tomorrow\n      if (parsed.isBefore(now)) {\n        parsed = parsed.add(1, 'day');\n      }\n      return parsed;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return null;\n}\n\n/**\n * Format relative time (e.g., \"in 1h 23m\")\n *\n * Uses dayjs for accurate time difference calculations.\n * Accepts both Date objects and dayjs objects.\n *\n * @param {Date|dayjs.Dayjs} resetDate - Date or dayjs object for reset time\n * @returns {string} - Formatted relative time string\n */\nexport function formatRelativeTime(resetDate) {\n  // Accept both Date objects and dayjs objects\n  let resetDayjs;\n  if (resetDate instanceof Date) {\n    resetDayjs = dayjs(resetDate);\n  } else if (dayjs.isDayjs(resetDate)) {\n    resetDayjs = resetDate;\n  } else {\n    return '';\n  }\n\n  if (!resetDayjs.isValid()) {\n    return '';\n  }\n\n  const now = dayjs();\n  const diffMs = resetDayjs.diff(now);\n\n  if (diffMs <= 0) {\n    return 'now';\n  }\n\n  const totalMinutes = Math.floor(diffMs / (1000 * 60));\n  const totalHours = Math.floor(totalMinutes / 60);\n  const totalDays = Math.floor(totalHours / 24);\n\n  const days = totalDays;\n  const hours = totalHours % 24;\n  const minutes = totalMinutes % 60;\n\n  const parts = [];\n  if (days > 0) parts.push(`${days}d`);\n  if (hours > 0) parts.push(`${hours}h`);\n  if (minutes > 0 || parts.length === 0) parts.push(`${minutes}m`);\n\n  return `in ${parts.join(' ')}`;\n}\n\n/**\n * Format reset time with relative time and UTC time\n * Example: \"in 1h 23m (Jan 15, 7:00 AM UTC)\"\n *\n * Uses dayjs for proper timezone conversion to UTC.\n *\n * @param {string} resetTime - Time string in format \"HH:MM AM/PM\" or \"Mon DD, HH:MM AM/PM\"\n * @param {string|null} timezone - Optional IANA timezone (e.g., \"Europe/Berlin\")\n * @returns {string} - Formatted string with relative and absolute UTC time\n */\nexport function formatResetTimeWithRelative(resetTime, timezone = null) {\n  if (!resetTime) {\n    return resetTime;\n  }\n\n  const resetDate = parseResetTime(resetTime, timezone);\n  if (!resetDate) {\n    // If we can't parse it, return the original time\n    return resetTime;\n  }\n\n  const relativeTime = formatRelativeTime(resetDate);\n\n  // Convert to UTC and format\n  const utcDate = resetDate.utc();\n  const utcTimeStr = utcDate.format('MMM D, h:mm A [UTC]');\n\n  return `${relativeTime} lines.push('Please wait for the limit to reset.');\n  }\n\n  if (sessionId && resumeCommand) {\n    lines.push('');\n    lines.push(`📌 Session ID: ${sessionId}`);\n    lines.push('');\n usage limit error and is in JSON format\n * Useful for parsing structured error responses\n *\n * @param {string} line - Line to check\n * @returns {Object|null} - Parsed JSON object if valid, null otherwise\n */\nexport function parseUsageLimitJson(line) {\n  try {\n    const data = JSON.parse(line);\n\n    // Check for error in JSON\n    if (data.type === 'error' && data.message) {\n      if (isUsageLimitError(data.message)) {\n        return {\n          type: 'error',\n          message: data.message,\n          limitInfo: detectUsageLimit(data.message),\n        };\n      }\n    }\n\n 'turn.failed',\n          message: data.error.message,\n          limitInfo: detectUsageLimit(data.error.message),\n        };\n      }\n    }\n\n    return null;\n  } catch {\n    return null;\n  }\n}\n",

          "content": "# Case Study: Issue #1296 - False Positive Error Detection for `--tool agent`\n\n## Executive Summary\n\n**Issue:** [#1296 - False positive error detection for `--tool agent`](https://github.com/link-assistant/hive-mind/issues/1296)\n\n**Root Cause:** The error detection logic in `src/agent.lib.mjs` has a fallback pattern matching mechanism (lines 790-837) that detects `\"type\": \"error\"` or `\"type\": \"step_error\"` patterns in the raw output string. This fallback triggers even when the agent has successfully completed (exit code 0, `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"`), causing false positive error reporting.\n\n**Specific Trigger:** When an agent encounters a timeout error during execution (e.g., `\"The operation timed out.\"`), the error event is logged to output. Even if the agent recovers from this error and successfully completes (indicated by `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"` and exit code 0), the fallback pattern matching still detects the error message in the full output and reports it as a failure.\n\n**Impact:**\n1. Valid agent executions are incorrectly flagged as failures\n2. Misleading error messages despite successful task completion\n3. False negatives in CI/CD pipelines\n\n**Fix Status:** Solution identified and implementation ready.\n\n---\n\n## Timeline / Sequence of Events\n\nBased on the logs provided in the issue:\n\n### Event 1: Agent Executes Successfully\n\n- **Time:** 2026-02-15T00:01:54.716Z\n- **Type:** `step_finish`\n- **Session ID:** `ses_3a3d83adfffeCkqmlFB4bV7c68`\n- **Details:**\n  ```json\n  {\n    \"type\": \"step_finish\",\n    \"timestamp\": 1771113714714,\n    \"part\": {\n      \"id\": \"prt_c5e9a91a5001VWYa1WPGDHs2rd\",\n      \"type\": \"step-finish\",\n      \"reason\": \"stop\",\n      \"tokens\": {\n        \"input\": 22868,\n        \"output\": 159,\n        \"reasoning\": 0,\n        \"cache\": { \"read\": 0, \"write\": 0 }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  ```\n- **Significance:** This is a clear marker of successful completion. The `reason: \"stop\"` indicates normal termination.\n\n### Event 2: False Positive Error Detection (BUG)\n\n- **Time:** 2026-02-15T00:01:54.979Z\n- **Location:** `src/agent.lib.mjs` - fallback pattern matching\n- **Pattern Matched:** String pattern in full output containing `\"The operation timed out.\"`\n- **Error Generated:**\n  ```json\n  {\n    \"type\": \"error\",\n    \"exitCode\": 0,\n    \"errorDetectedInOutput\": true,\n    \"errorType\": \"AgentError\",\n    \"errorMatch\": \"The operation timed out.\",\n    \"message\": \"Agent reported error: The operation timed out.\",\n    \"sessionId\": null,\n    \"limitReached\": false,\n    \"limitResetTime\": null\n  }\n  ```\n\n**Critical Observation:**\n- Exit code is 0 (success)\n- `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"` was emitted (success marker)\n- Error was detected via \"fallback pattern match\" - meaning JSON parsing failed and raw string scanning found error patterns\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause Analysis\n\n### Primary Issue: Fallback Pattern Matching Not Respecting Success Markers\n\nThe error detection code at `src/agent.lib.mjs:790-837` contains fallback pattern matching:\n\n```javascript\n// Issue #1258: Fallback pattern match for error detection\n// When JSON parsing fails (e.g., multi-line pretty-printed JSON in logs),\n// we need to detect error patterns in the raw output string\n// Issue #1290: Skip fallback when agent completed successfully with exit code 0\n// The fallback can cause false positives when error events (like AI_JSONParseError)\n// appear in the output but the agent recovered and completed successfully\nif (!outputError.detected && !streamingErrorDetected && !(exitCode === 0 && agentCompletedSuccessfully)) {\n  // Check for error type patterns in raw output (handles pretty-printed JSON)\n  const errorTypePatterns = [\n    { pattern: '\"type\": \"error\"', type: 'AgentError' },\n    { pattern: '\"type\":\"error\"', type: 'AgentError' },\n    { pattern: '\"type\": \"step_error\"', type: 'AgentStepError' },\n    { pattern: '\"type\":\"step_error\"', type: 'AgentStepError' },\n  ];\n  // ...\n}\n```\n\nThe issue is that the condition `!(exitCode === 0 && agentCompletedSuccessfully)` depends on `agentCompletedSuccessfully` being set to `true`. However, `agentCompletedSuccessfully` is only set when specific completion events are detected:\n\n```javascript\n// Issue #1276: Detect successful completion events\nif (data.type === 'session.idle' || (data.type === 'log' && data.message === 'exiting loop')) {\n  agentCompletedSuccessfully = true;\n}\n```\n\n**The bug:** The `step_finish` event with `reason: \"stop\"` is NOT being tracked as a success marker. This means when an agent completes via `step_finish`, the `agentCompletedSuccessfully` flag remains `false`, allowing the fallback pattern matching to trigger.\n\n### Secondary Issue: Error Events Persisted in Output\n\nWhen the agent encounters a timeout error during execution:\n1. The agent emits an error event (`type: \"error\"`, `error: \"The operation timed out.\"`)\n2. The agent may recover and continue (retry logic)\n3. The agent eventually completes successfully (`step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"`)\n4. The full output contains BOTH the error event AND the success event\n5. The fallback pattern matching scans the FULL output and finds the error pattern\n\n### Why Issue #1276 Fix Didn't Fully Work\n\nIssue #1276 added tracking for `agentCompletedSuccessfully` using `session.idle` and `\"exiting loop\"` log messages. However:\n\n1. Not all agent completion scenarios emit these specific events\n2. The `step_finish` event with `reason: \"stop\"` is a more reliable indicator but was not included\n3. The agent in this case likely completed via `step_finish` without emitting `session.idle`\n\n---\n\n## Evidence from Logs\n\n### Success Marker (Present)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"type\": \"step_finish\",\n  \"part\": {\n    \"type\": \"step-finish\",\n    \"reason\": \"stop\"  // <-- This is a success marker\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Error Pattern Matched by Fallback (False Positive)\n\n```\n[2026-02-15T00:01:54.979Z] [WARNING] ⚠️  Error event detected via fallback pattern match: The operation timed out.\n```\n\nThe warning explicitly states \"via fallback pattern match\", indicating that:\n1. Streaming error detection didn't catch this as an error (correct - because it was followed by recovery)\n2. JSON parsing-based detection didn't catch it as an error (correct - because step_finish showed success)\n3. The fallback raw string scanning DID catch it (incorrect - false positive)\n\n---\n\n## Related Issues and Prior Art\n\n### In This Repository (hive-mind)\n\n1. **Issue #886** - False positive error detection for `--agent tool`\n   - Similar root cause: pattern matching in successful tool outputs\n   - Solution: Trust exit code, simplified error detection to JSON-only\n\n2. **Issue #873** - Phantom error detection for `--tool agent`\n   - Similar root cause: scanning all output including tool content\n   - Solution: Parse JSON structure, skip completed tool outputs\n\n3. **Issue #1276** - Added `agentCompletedSuccessfully` tracking\n   - Partial fix: Added tracking for `session.idle` and `\"exiting loop\"`\n   - Missed: `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"` as success marker\n\n4. **Issue #1290** - Skip fallback when agent completed successfully\n   - Condition added but depends on `agentCompletedSuccessfully` being set correctly\n\n### In Agent Repository (link-assistant/agent)\n\n1. **Issue #183** - `error: The operation timed out`\n   - The exact error message seen in this case\n   - Related to retry logic during rate limiting\n\n2. **Issue #154** - Unhandled AI_RetryError causes exit code 0 despite failure\n   - Related but opposite problem: agent NOT returning proper exit code\n   - This was fixed, but reveals agent's error handling evolution\n\n### External References\n\n1. [Vercel AI SDK - AI_RetryError](https://ai-sdk.dev/docs/reference/ai-sdk-errors/ai-retry-error)\n   - Agent uses Vercel AI SDK for retry logic\n   - Timeout configuration available: `totalMs`, `stepMs`, `chunkMs`\n\n2. [NDJSON Specification](https://jsonltools.com/ndjson-format-specification)\n   - Agent outputs NDJSON format\n   - Each line is an independent JSON object\n   - Error detection should parse line-by-line, not scan raw strings\n\n---\n\n## Proposed Solutions\n\n### Solution 1: Add `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"` as Success Marker (RECOMMENDED)\n\n**Approach:** Update the success detection logic to recognize `step_finish` events with `reason: \"stop\"` as successful completion.\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// In the streaming loop, add detection for step_finish success:\nif (data.type === 'step_finish' && data.part?.reason === 'stop') {\n  agentCompletedSuccessfully = true;\n}\n```\n\nThis should be added to both stdout and stderr processing blocks (around lines 615-650 and 682-715).\n\n**Pros:**\n- ✅ Addresses root cause directly\n- ✅ `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"` is a reliable success indicator\n- ✅ Minimal code change\n- ✅ Works with existing fallback protection at line 790\n\n**Cons:**\n- ⚠️ None significant\n\n### Solution 2: Disable Fallback Pattern Matching When Exit Code is 0\n\n**Approach:** If exit code is 0, trust it completely and skip fallback pattern matching.\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// Change condition at line 790 from:\nif (!outputError.detected && !streamingErrorDetected && !(exitCode === 0 && agentCompletedSuccessfully)) {\n// To:\nif (!outputError.detected && !streamingErrorDetected && exitCode !== 0) {\n```\n\n**Pros:**\n- ✅ Simple fix\n- ✅ Aligns with issue #886's principle: \"Trust the exit code\"\n\n**Cons:**\n- ⚠️ May miss errors if agent incorrectly exits with code 0 (issue #154 scenario)\n- ⚠️ Reduces defense-in-depth\n\n### Solution 3: Clear Error Detection When Success Markers Appear\n\n**Approach:** If a success marker (`step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"`) appears AFTER any error events, clear the error detection flags.\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// Already partially implemented at lines 762-773\n// Extend to also clear outputError.detected when step_finish success is seen:\nif (data.type === 'step_finish' && data.part?.reason === 'stop') {\n  agentCompletedSuccessfully = true;\n  // Clear any previously detected errors since agent recovered\n  streamingErrorDetected = false;\n  streamingErrorMessage = null;\n}\n```\n\n**Pros:**\n- ✅ Handles recovery scenarios correctly\n- ✅ More nuanced than just trusting exit code\n\n**Cons:**\n- ⚠️ Requires understanding temporal ordering of events\n\n---\n\n## Recommendation\n\n**Implement Solution 1 (Add `step_finish` Success Marker Detection)** as the primary fix.\n\n### Rationale:\n\n1. **It addresses the root cause:** The bug is that `agentCompletedSuccessfully` is not being set when agent completes via `step_finish`\n\n2. **It's minimal and low-risk:** Single addition to existing pattern detection\n\n3. **It maintains defense-in-depth:** The fallback pattern matching still works for genuine failures\n\n4. **It aligns with existing architecture:** The fix follows the pattern established in issue #1276\n\n### Implementation Plan:\n\n1. Add `step_finish` success detection to streaming loop (stdout processing)\n2. Add `step_finish` success detection to streaming loop (stderr processing)\n3. Add test case for this specific scenario\n4. The root cause is that the `agentCompletedSuccessfully` flag is not being set when the agent completes via `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"`.\n\nThe fix is straightforward: add detection for this specific success marker in the streaming loop. This will ensure that the fallback pattern matching at line 790 is correctly bypassed when the agent has successfully completed.\n\n### Key Insight\n\nThe issue statement captures this perfectly:\n> \"So if we have clear marker of success in the output, we can drop all error detection.\"\n\nThe `step_finish` event with `reason: \"stop\"` IS that clear marker.     "type": "create",
    "filePath": "/tmp/gh-issue-solver-1771161896687/docs/case-studies/issue-1296/README.md",
    "content": "# Case Study: Issue #1296 - False Positive Error Detection for `--tool agent`\n\n## Executive Summary\n\n**Issue:** [#1296 - False positive error detection for `--tool agent`](https://github.com/link-assistant/hive-mind/issues/1296)\n\n**Root Cause:** The error detection logic in `src/agent.lib.mjs` has a fallback pattern matching mechanism (lines 790-837) that detects `\"type\": \"error\"` or `\"type\": \"step_error\"` patterns in the raw output string. This fallback triggers even when the agent has successfully completed (exit code 0, `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"`), causing false positive error reporting.\n\n**Specific Trigger:** When an agent encounters a timeout error during execution (e.g., `\"The operation timed out.\"`), the error event is logged to output. Even if the agent recovers from this error and successfully completes (indicated by `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"` and exit code 0), the fallback pattern matching still detects the error message in the full output and reports it as a failure.\n\n**Impact:**\n1. Valid agent executions are incorrectly flagged as failures\n2. Misleading error messages despite successful task completion\n3. False negatives in CI/CD pipelines\n\n**Fix Status:** Solution identified and implementation ready.\n\n---\n\n## Timeline / Sequence of Events\n\nBased on the logs provided in the issue:\n\n### Event 1: Agent Executes Successfully\n\n- **Time:** 2026-02-15T00:01:54.716Z\n- **Type:** `step_finish`\n- **Session ID:** `ses_3a3d83adfffeCkqmlFB4bV7c68`\n- **Details:**\n  ```json\n  {\n    \"type\": \"step_finish\",\n    \"timestamp\": 1771113714714,\n    \"part\": {\n      \"id\": \"prt_c5e9a91a5001VWYa1WPGDHs2rd\",\n      \"type\": \"step-finish\",\n      \"reason\": \"stop\",\n      \"tokens\": {\n        \"input\": 22868,\n        \"output\": 159,\n        \"reasoning\": 0,\n        \"cache\": { \"read\": 0, \"write\": 0 }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  ```\n- **Significance:** This is a clear marker of successful completion. The `reason: \"stop\"` indicates normal termination.\n\n### Event 2: False Positive Error Detection (BUG)\n\n- **Time:** 2026-02-15T00:01:54.979Z\n- **Location:** `src/agent.lib.mjs` - fallback pattern matching\n- **Pattern Matched:** String pattern in full output containing `\"The operation timed out.\"`\n- **Error Generated:**\n  ```json\n  {\n    \"type\": \"error\",\n    \"exitCode\": 0,\n    \"errorDetectedInOutput\": true,\n    \"errorType\": \"AgentError\",\n    \"errorMatch\": \"The operation timed out.\",\n    \"message\": \"Agent reported error: The operation timed out.\",\n    \"sessionId\": null,\n    \"limitReached\": false,\n    \"limitResetTime\": null\n  }\n  ```\n\n**Critical Observation:**\n- Exit code is 0 (success)\n- `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"` was emitted (success marker)\n- Error was detected via \"fallback pattern match\" - meaning JSON parsing failed and raw string scanning found error patterns\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause Analysis\n\n### Primary Issue: Fallback Pattern Matching Not Respecting Success Markers\n\nThe error detection code at `src/agent.lib.mjs:790-837` contains fallback pattern matching:\n\n```javascript\n// Issue #1258: Fallback pattern match for error detection\n// When JSON parsing fails (e.g., multi-line pretty-printed JSON in logs),\n// we need to detect error patterns in the raw output string\n// Issue #1290: Skip fallback when agent completed successfully with exit code 0\n// The fallback can cause false positives when error events (like AI_JSONParseError)\n// appear in the output but the agent recovered and completed successfully\nif (!outputError.detected && !streamingErrorDetected && !(exitCode === 0 && agentCompletedSuccessfully)) {\n  // Check for error type patterns in raw output (handles pretty-printed JSON)\n  const errorTypePatterns = [\n    { pattern: '\"type\": \"error\"', type: 'AgentError' },\n    { pattern: '\"type\":\"error\"', type: 'AgentError' },\n    { pattern: '\"type\": \"step_error\"', type: 'AgentStepError' },\n    { pattern: '\"type\":\"step_error\"', type: 'AgentStepError' },\n  ];\n  // ...\n}\n```\n\nThe issue is that the condition `!(exitCode === 0 && agentCompletedSuccessfully)` depends on `agentCompletedSuccessfully` being set to `true`. However, `agentCompletedSuccessfully` is only set when specific completion events are detected:\n\n```javascript\n// Issue #1276: Detect successful completion events\nif (data.type === 'session.idle' || (data.type === 'log' && data.message === 'exiting loop')) {\n  agentCompletedSuccessfully = true;\n}\n```\n\n**The bug:** The `step_finish` event with `reason: \"stop\"` is NOT being tracked as a success marker. This means when an agent completes via `step_finish`, the `agentCompletedSuccessfully` flag remains `false`, allowing the fallback pattern matching to trigger.\n\n### Secondary Issue: Error Events Persisted in Output\n\nWhen the agent encounters a timeout error during execution:\n1. The agent emits an error event (`type: \"error\"`, `error: \"The operation timed out.\"`)\n2. The agent may recover and continue (retry logic)\n3. The agent eventually completes successfully (`step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"`)\n4. The full output contains BOTH the error event AND the success event\n5. The fallback pattern matching scans the FULL output and finds the error pattern\n\n### Why Issue #1276 Fix Didn't Fully Work\n\nIssue #1276 added tracking for `agentCompletedSuccessfully` using `session.idle` and `\"exiting loop\"` log messages. However:\n\n1. Not all agent completion scenarios emit these specific events\n2. The `step_finish` event with `reason: \"stop\"` is a more reliable indicator but was not included\n3. The agent in this case likely completed via `step_finish` without emitting `session.idle`\n\n---\n\n## Evidence from Logs\n\n### Success Marker (Present)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"type\": \"step_finish\",\n  \"part\": {\n    \"type\": \"step-finish\",\n    \"reason\": \"stop\"  // <-- This is a success marker\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Error Pattern Matched by Fallback (False Positive)\n\n```\n[2026-02-15T00:01:54.979Z] [WARNING] ⚠️  Error event detected via fallback pattern match: The operation timed out.\n```\n\nThe warning explicitly states \"via fallback pattern match\", indicating that:\n1. Streaming error detection didn't catch this as an error (correct - because it was followed by recovery)\n2. JSON parsing-based detection didn't catch it as an error (correct - because step_finish showed success)\n3. The fallback raw string scanning DID catch it (incorrect - false positive)\n\n---\n\n## Related Issues and Prior Art\n\n### In This Repository (hive-mind)\n\n1. **Issue #886** - False positive error detection for `--agent tool`\n   - Similar root cause: pattern matching in successful tool outputs\n   - Solution: Trust exit code, simplified error detection to JSON-only\n\n2. **Issue #873** - Phantom error detection for `--tool agent`\n   - Similar root cause: scanning all output including tool content\n   - Solution: Parse JSON structure, skip completed tool outputs\n\n3. **Issue #1276** - Added `agentCompletedSuccessfully` tracking\n   - Partial fix: Added tracking for `session.idle` and `\"exiting loop\"`\n   - Missed: `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"` as success marker\n\n4. **Issue #1290** - Skip fallback when agent completed successfully\n   - Condition added but depends on `agentCompletedSuccessfully` being set correctly\n\n### In Agent Repository (link-assistant/agent)\n\n1. **Issue #183** - `error: The operation timed out`\n   - The exact error message seen in this case\n   - Related to retry logic during rate limiting\n\n2. **Issue #154** - Unhandled AI_RetryError causes exit code 0 despite failure\n   - Related but opposite problem: agent NOT returning proper exit code\n   - This was fixed, but reveals agent's error handling evolution\n\n### External References\n\n1. [Vercel AI SDK - AI_RetryError](https://ai-sdk.dev/docs/reference/ai-sdk-errors/ai-retry-error)\n   - Agent uses Vercel AI SDK for retry logic\n   - Timeout configuration available: `totalMs`, `stepMs`, `chunkMs`\n\n2. [NDJSON Specification](https://jsonltools.com/ndjson-format-specification)\n   - Agent outputs NDJSON format\n   - Each line is an independent JSON object\n   - Error detection should parse line-by-line, not scan raw strings\n\n---\n\n## Proposed Solutions\n\n### Solution 1: Add `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"` as Success Marker (RECOMMENDED)\n\n**Approach:** Update the success detection logic to recognize `step_finish` events with `reason: \"stop\"` as successful completion.\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// In the streaming loop, add detection for step_finish success:\nif (data.type === 'step_finish' && data.part?.reason === 'stop') {\n  agentCompletedSuccessfully = true;\n}\n```\n\nThis should be added to both stdout and stderr processing blocks (around lines 615-650 and 682-715).\n\n**Pros:**\n- ✅ Addresses root cause directly\n- ✅ `step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"` is a reliable success indicator\n- ✅ Minimal code change\n- ✅ Works with existing fallback protection at line 790\n\n**Cons:**\n- ⚠️ None significant\n\n### Solution 2: Disable Fallback Pattern Matching When Exit Code is 0\n\n**Approach:** If exit code is 0, trust it completely and skip fallback pattern matching.\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// Change condition at line 790 from:\nif (!outputError.detected && !streamingErrorDetected && !(exitCode === 0 && agentCompletedSuccessfully)) {\n// To:\nif (!outputError.detected && !streamingErrorDetected && exitCode !== 0) {\n```\n\n**Pros:**\n- ✅ Simple fix\n- ✅ Aligns with issue #886's principle: \"Trust the exit code\"\n\n**Cons:**\n- ⚠️ May miss errors if agent incorrectly exits with code 0 (issue #154 scenario)\n- ⚠️ Reduces defense-in-depth\n\n### Solution 3: Clear Error Detection When Success Markers Appear\n\n**Approach:** If a success marker (`step_finish` with `reason: \"stop\"`) appears AFTER any error events, clear the error detection flags.\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```javascript\n// Already partially implemented at lines 762-773\n// Extend to also clear outputError.detected when step_finish success is seen:\nif (data.type === 'step_finish' && data.part?.reason === 'stop') {\n  agentCompletedSuccessfully = true;\n  // Clear any previously detected errors since agent recovered\n  streamingErrorDetected = false;\n  streamingErrorMessage = null;\n}\n```\n\n**Pros:**\n- ✅ Handles recovery scenarios correctly\n- ✅ More nuanced than just trusting exit code\n\n**Cons:**\n- ⚠️ Requires understanding temporal ordering of events\n\n---\n\n## Recommendation\n\n**Implement Solution 1 (Add `step_finish` Success Marker Detection)** as the primary fix.\n\n### Rationale:\n\n1. **It addresses the root cause:** The bug is that `agentCompletedSuccessfully` is not being set when agent completes via `step_finish`\n\n2. **It's minimal and low-risk:** Single addition to existing pattern detection\n\n3. **It maintains defense-in-depth:** The fallback pattern matching still works for genuine failures\n\n4. **It aligns with existing architecture:** The fix follows the pattern established in issue #1276\n\n### Implementation Plan:\n\n1. Add `step_finish` success detection to streaming loop (stdout processing)\n2. Add `step_finish` success detection to streaming loop (stderr processing)\n3. Add test case for this specific scenario\n4. Update case study documentation\n\n---\n\n## Test Cases\n\n### Test Case 1: Current Bug Scenario (Issue #1296)\n\n- **Input:** Agent encounters timeout error, recovers, completes with `step_finish` reason `stop`\n- **Expected:** No error reported (exit code 0, success marker present)\n- **Current Result:** ❌ False positive error detected via fallback\n- **After Fix:** ✅ No error detected\n\n### Test Case 2: Genuine Failure\n\n- **Input:** Agent encounters error, does NOT recover, exits with code 1\n- **Expected:** Error detected and reported\n- **Current Result:** ✅ Correctly detected\n- **After Fix:** ✅ Still detected\n\n### Test Case 3: Timeout Without Recovery\n\n- **Input:** Agent encounters timeout error, fails to recover, exits with code 1\n- **Expected:** Error detected and reported\n- **Current Result:** ✅ Correctly detected\n- **After Fix:** ✅ Still detected\n\n---\n\n## Files to Modify\n\n| File                                   | Change                                                      |\n| -------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------- |\n| `src/agent.lib.mjs`                    | Add `step_finish` success detection in streaming loops      |\n| `tests/test-agent-error-detection.mjs` | Add test case for timeout recovery scenario                 |\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThis issue is a continuation of the false positive error detection pattern addressed in issues #873, #886, #1276, and #1290.
